Guanghua and Russian Oil Amend Contract

Eliminating the Management System and Changing to a Purchase and Sale System

Yesterday, it was heard that Guanghua Petroleum Company in Shanghai and Russian Oil had amended their contract. A reporter from this newspaper inquired with the person in charge of Guanghua, whose reply was as follows:

Business Situation

Guanghua started business in 1929, purchasing and selling American oil. With the support of Chinese people, the business was very good. In 1931, Russian oil arrived in Shanghai. In order to avoid competition, Guanghua signed a management contract with them on August 25th, which was implemented from January 1932. In 1933, oil companies had misunderstandings, and oil prices fell, resulting in losses for everyone. However, Chinese users benefited greatly from the low prices. Guanghua only earned commissions under the management system, so it was not affected by the drop in oil prices. Although the profit was less, there was no loss. Since this spring, oil companies have been sincerely cooperating and negotiating with each other, and oil prices have gradually recovered. The Russian side also has no intention of monopolizing the market, so it agreed to Guanghua's request to cancel the management contract on August 25th and amend it to a oil purchase contract. From then on, business is completely under Guanghua's independent responsibility, restoring the system of 1931. This is the actual situation in recent days.

My Personal Thoughts

As for my personal feelings about this oil price competition, I have three thoughts: (1) The British and American oil companies and Soviet oil companies are willing to make significant sacrifices to compete for the market, and their spirit is admirable. (2) Soviet Russia and China, just after resuming trade, were also able to sacrifice huge losses to compete with British and American oil companies, and the market they won was given to our Chinese merchants as managers. Their great spirit in business is also respectable. (3) In recent years, China's banking industry has paid more and more attention to supporting industry. Even during the period of oil price competition in the past two years, Guanghua has been trusted by various banks and given strong support. Their concern for maintaining industry is truly commendable. As for the operation of the kerosene business in the future, it will be more difficult than before, firstly because tariffs are heavier than before, and secondly because tax-free local oil is rampant in the market. If the government does not prohibit local oil, the sales of various oil companies will be reduced, and the government's tariff revenue will also be affected.

Customs Patrol Ship Annihilates Pirates

Pirate Ship Sunk, Six Hostages Rescued

The Jianghai Customs patrol ship "Wenxing" engaged in a fierce battle with pirates around one hundred miles south of the Wusongkou front the day before yesterday. As a result, two of the ten pirates were killed, three drowned, and five were captured. Three of the captured criminals were already injured at the time of capture. Of the ten hostages held captive on the pirate ship, six were rescued, one of whom was injured by a bullet. The remaining four hostages drowned when the pirate ship sank. On the customs sailors' side, only one person went missing and three were slightly injured. The ship returned to Shanghai at 11:45 PM the night before last and was docked at buoy number 18 in the Huangpu River. According to the report from the ship's sailors, the course of the battle with the pirates was as follows: the ship left port around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, as usual, to conduct a ten-day anti-smuggling patrol. This trip was originally intended to patrol from Shanghai along the coast to Ningbo and the North Saddle Island area. After sailing out, just as it reached about one hundred miles south of Wusongkou, near the Fu Port area of Zhejiang, the ship's officers immediately discovered a large sand boat parked next to another sand boat, with several sampans parked near the beach. Because the customs patrol personnel at the time saw that the large sand boat was heavily loaded, they became suspicious and sent a small boat, led by Captain Qiaoxi, with three Chinese sailors to investigate. Unexpectedly, as they boarded the sand boat to conduct a search, they were shot at by the pirates. One sailor was injured. At that time, outnumbered and outgunned, they retreated together. The injured sailor went missing due to being injured and unable to escape in time. The Customs "Wenxing" patrol ship opened fire and returned fire at the sand boat, and thus the fierce battle began. The patrol ship decided to sink the sand boat and swept the hull with machine guns. Before long, the hull was riddled with holes and sank. Thereupon, the pirates were captured. The ten hostages who were kidnapped were all fishermen. Except for those who drowned due to the ship sinking and those who died from being shot, the rest were rescued. After the incident, a thorough search for the injured sailor yielded no results. He probably drowned while trying to escape.

Landlord Coerces Civilians, Forbidding Vegetable Vendors to Peddle

Small Vendors Suddenly Lose Their Livelihood

Residents All Complain Bitterly

Lane 3 of Hengfeng Lane, Hengsheng Lane, and Sida Lane on Shigaota Road are operated by the Hengfeng, Hengsheng, and Hengli Companies, with over 1,500 households. Traditionally, the company has always allowed vegetable vendors carrying shoulder poles to enter the lane to peddle, but with the restriction that it be limited to between 8:00 AM and 11:00 AM. Most residents found it quite convenient. Unexpectedly, the landlord of Hengfeng Lane, surnamed Zhou, at the request of a few residents who owned private chartered cars, believing that the comings and goings of vegetable vendors obstructed traffic, suddenly presented a request to the competent Third Section of the Fifth District, starting from the 1st of this month, to prohibit vegetable vendors from entering and exiting. Considering that most of the tenants in the three lanes belong to the common people class, and the vegetable market is on Tiantong Road, about four stops away, they suddenly heard that the landlord, disregarding the convenience of the residents and the livelihood of the small vendors, rose up in resistance. Currently, the tenants of the three lanes are all extremely resentful and will unite to issue a serious warning to the landlords of the three lanes. At the same time, over a thousand small vendors, forced by their livelihood and suddenly cut off from their sales channels, gathered from various trades, believing that the Third Section of the Fifth District did not consider the interests of the public and only listened to the landlord's orders, which was particularly unsatisfactory. The reporter went to Sida Lane to investigate the truth of the matter and saw that the residents in the lane were all filled with resentment, saying that Zhou, the landlord of Hengfeng Lane, because he owned a private chartered car and went in and out every day, was jealous of the comings and goings of the small vendors, and invited the landlords of Hengsheng and Sida Lanes to strongly request the competent authority to interfere. The Third Section of the Fifth District, without considering the lives of the small vendors and the habits of the residents, rashly ordered a prohibition. It is said that the tenants of the three lanes have successively reduced rents along Shigaota Road, but the three lanes of Hengfeng, Hengsheng, and Sida not only ignored it but also sought personal gain and oppressed the civilians, and will have considerable methods to deal with it, etc.

New Method of Enticing Gambling by Con Artists

Using Rhodesian Foreign Buttons as Gambling Tools

Dividing into Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Enter Treasure, and Exit Treasure

—Liu Dinggui and Con Artists Detained Together—

Liu Dinggui, a native of Tongzhou residing at No. 66 opposite Puyutang outside the Dananmen in the Nanshi district, published an advertisement in the Xinwen Daily last month, stating that he had twelve buildings built on rented land in the Xiqiao area, with eighteen years remaining on the lease, and was willing to sell them at a low price. If anyone was interested, they could contact him. The next day, a person named Jin Shutang sent a letter to Liu, saying that someone wanted to buy the house and requested him to contact him at Room 415 on the upper floor of the Changsha Merchants' Warehouse in the Diandang Street on Gongguan Road, etc. Liu then went to the appointment. When he arrived, he saw a signboard of Yufengtai Zhuang hanging at the door of the room. He entered and saw Jin seated. As they were conversing, a person surnamed Mo came to Jin and asked for 500 yuan. Jin immediately handed over 500 yuan in cash to Mo. After he left, Jin said to Liu, "The Mo family has millions of dollars in assets and is addicted to gambling. We might as well raise a gambling stake of 20,000 yuan and pretend to gamble with Mo. In secret, we can agree in advance that we can win tens of thousands of yuan from him. It's as easy as pie." Liu was deeply convinced and agreed. He went home to retrieve 200 yuan and went to the Changsha Merchants' Warehouse again. Jin claimed that he had already raised 10,000 yuan, using Rhodesian foreign buttons as gambling tools. The dealer would hold a handful of buttons in his hand and ask the gamblers to guess the number, called "grabbing the spread." The dealer and his accomplices would agree in advance that the dealer would hold a chopstick, dial the Rhodesian buttons, and extend his finger to press on the chopstick, using one to four as a secret code, which would indicate the number of buttons in the palm, divided into Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Enter Treasure, and Exit Treasure. Jin arranged everything and then ordered Liu Dinggui to be the dealer. Liu then sat down and followed the procedure. However, Jin and the gamblers present were all accomplices. Therefore, in the blink of an eye, Liu had lost 200 yuan in cash and still owed over 5,000 yuan to Jin. Liu was heartbroken. Jin then ordered Liu to go home and raise more money, hoping to gamble again on the 31st to recoup his losses. Liu went home disappointed and began to realize that Jin and others had set up a gambling scam. He reported to the French police for investigation. Inspector Jin Jiulin, detective Jiang Changwen, and detectives Dai Rongji, Jin Bingwen, Zuo Qihong, etc., went and arrested Wanren Yan Songchen (resident of No. 10 Xinzha Road) and Wang Shoushan (nickname Huang Da Liuzi, resident of No. 145 Meibaike Road). After interrogation by the police chief, it was deemed that the plaintiff Liu Dinggui had participated in gambling, which was also inappropriate, and ordered them to be detained together. Romanian Man Privately Alters Alien Passport

Possession of Handgun Also Unlicensed

Prosecuted After Investigation by Police

Romanian Mouxiyaluo Poersike, who worked as an engineer in Shanghai, lived at 115 Fookaison Road in the French Concession. The alien passport he held was issued by the Canadian government in English, but the name and nationality on the passport were inconsistent with Mouxiyaluo's. After the police of the Public Concession investigated and found that the passport was indeed forged by Mouxiyaluo, they reported it to the First District Court and issued an arrest warrant. At 3:30 PM on the 25th of last month, Chief Patrol Pappu caught Mouxiyaluo on Fookaison Road and found a "Shaoyou" brand automatic pistol, six bullets, and a passport in his car. He was handed over to the First District Court and ordered to be detained for investigation. Now, according to the police's investigation with the British Consulate in Shanghai, the results confirmed that the passport had indeed been altered by Mouxiyaluo, and that the weapons he possessed were also unlicensed. Therefore, according to Article 233 of the Criminal Law on forging documents and Article 2 of the Regulations on the Prohibition of Military Firearms, a public prosecution was filed. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian Hongye ordered the defendant to be brought to court for interrogation. After the police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the case, the court immediately interrogated the defendant. However, he denied that the passport was forged by him, but stated that due to certain entanglements when he went to Italy, he changed the name on the passport. As for the failure to register the firearms, he argued that his pistol was placed in the car at the time, and the car was parked in the French Concession of Fookaison Road. Since it was neither hidden on his person nor did he step into the Public Concession, he did not need to register, etc. However, the investigating Chief Patrol testified that the defendant was arrested on the Public Concession side. After the police lawyer and the defendant's defense lawyer debated successively, Judge Qian ordered the defendant to pay 3,000 yuan bail and wait for the verdict next Wednesday.

Chen Xiangtao Discusses the Rapid Development of Tourism in Qingdao

Tourists Send More Than Ten Million Yuan in Remittances

Mayor Shen's Prosperity Plan Succeeds

Mr. Chen Xiangtao, the president of the China Travel Service, went to Qingdao twice this time due to company affairs and deeply felt that Qingdao will definitely become a tourism center in the future. The reporter visited him yesterday and received the following report on Qingdao's tourism construction: "Around the summer of this year, I went to Qingdao twice on business. Observing from the perspective of a travel operator, I deeply feel that Qingdao will definitely become a tourism and sightseeing center in the future, which is my intention. I cannot help but say a word about the efforts of the Qingdao authorities to prosper the city. Judging from the records of our company, I can give a brief overview of the progress of various summer resorts in the past two or three years: The mountain area is best represented by Guling because Chairman Chiang held meetings and officer training classes there, with dignitaries and ladies flocking there. Mogan Mountain suffered from drought this year, which inevitably affected tourism. In terms of seaside resorts, Beidaihe was affected by the Northeast Incident, and tourism declined far less than in the past. On the contrary, Qingdao saw a sharp increase in tourists during the peak summer season, with even the remaining houses in the city being completely rented out. Thousands of people went to the seaside to escape the heat. A certain local bank told me that American naval personnel alone remitted more than two million yuan to Qingdao in one summer. If we consider all tourists, the amount of money brought to Qingdao must have exceeded ten million yuan. The travel industry is originally a new type of industry, and the amount of investment it attracts is considerable. Therefore, internationally, it has long been regarded as an 'invisible export.' In our country, this industry is still in its infancy, and few people know about it. I deeply believe that it can attract more attention in the future in order to seek its development and advancement. Qingdao's summer resort benefits greatly from its natural landscape. The clear water and white sand complement each other, and the scenery of Laoshan is pleasant. However, without the efforts of Mayor Shen Honglie and the gentlemen of the municipal government, it would be almost impossible to develop Qingdao into a travel center. Here are the most notable points: Last year, under the leadership of Commander Shen, the Qingdao Prosperity Promotion Association was established, with the aim of developing the travel industry. Twenty-five local celebrities were invited to be members, and employees were hired to handle daily affairs. Two types of magazines, one in Chinese and one in English, were published. The English one was named 'Qingdao's Outlook,' and the Chinese one was called 'Qingdao Pictorial,' published every two weeks. In addition, a Chinese-English tour guide manual was published, with five copies in a set, and distributed free of charge. In addition to publishing books and newspapers, the association also worked hard on transportation, public safety, and entertainment. As a result, the public transportation companies, which used to have irregular routes, vehicles, and fare collection, and inadequate equipment, were merged into a large organization called the Xinren Society under the strict supervision of the municipal government. On the one hand, it provides satisfactory service to the public, and on the other hand, it gives the shareholders of each company a reasonable profit. The association also urged the theaters to improve their hygiene equipment and sent personnel to inspect them from time to time. In order to increase the interest of tourists, the association raised funds to build four steamers, four yachts, and eleven rowing boats, which were rented to guests at low prices. Road and vehicle traffic were improved, and in October, the traffic was changed to the left-hand side for the convenience of tourists. In terms of public safety, the Public Security Bureau is responsible, and the whole city is worry-free. Moreover, due to the strict household registration investigation, bandits and thieves have nowhere to hide in Qingdao, and it is even more difficult to use their skills. The sea inhabitants who are disgusted by being in the company of镖师镖师 and cannot help but have them protect them can be freed from the shackles and live freely and happily in Qingdao. Good roads are being built near Qingdao at any time. Most of the roads in and out of the city are paved with asphalt, so it is very comfortable to drive around Qingdao. This year, the China Travel Service has obtained special convenience in Qingdao, using low-dust fees to transport cars to the port. For example, if customers transport cars from Shanghai to Qingdao, they only need to pay the travel agency a deposit of 50 yuan. When the ship arrives at the port, if they notify in advance, the company will send someone to the pier with the car license. As soon as it is properly hung up, the car can drive straight away. At the same time, customs inspection and registration procedures are handled by the company, so that the tourists can just sit back and enjoy the results. Recently, many new roads have been built, connecting with Qingdao and reaching major cities. It takes eight hours by car from Qingdao to Jixian County, and nine, five, and six hours to Huangxian, Shahe, and Haiyang, respectively. There is also a specially built road to Laoshan, which can be reached directly. It takes about an hour by car. There are many flat roads in the mountains, which are very suitable for walking or riding in sedan chairs. The best impression tourists have after arriving in Qingdao is not only the clean streets and complete public buildings that are constantly being cleaned up, but also the ability of Mayor Shen to solve the problem of beggars, which is different from other cities in the country that are full of鸠形鹊鸠形鹊. There are a total of 580 beggars in Qingdao, but they are never seen on the streets. This is because the mayor cares about the poor and drives them all to a small island called Dongdao. The government pays for them to work separately. Among them, 300 people are engaged in road construction, 30 crippled beggars make gunpowder boxes, and the remaining 200 people are sent to the reformatory to learn various skills, such as shoemaking, carpet weaving, iron forging, spinning, rope making, printing, etc. In addition to working, they also have to take classes for two hours every day. Those who have reformed and learned a skill are allowed to make a living on their own and become healthy citizens. From this, it can be seen that Mayor Shen's attention to society and the happiness of citizens is not neglected because of their humble status. Mayor Shen treats the people like his own children and is loved by all the citizens of Qingdao. I believe that I am humble and dare not sing the praises of the mayor's achievements, but from the standpoint of a travel agency, Mayor Shen's support and maintenance of the travel industry is truly appreciated."

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Strictly Prohibits Infanticide and Damage to Children's Corpses

Offenders Will Be Sentenced to Death or Life Imprisonment

Ignorant People Should Not Test the Law

Wu Xingya, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, issued a public notice yesterday to strictly prohibit the acts of cutting infant corpses and chopping sick children, which have been found in remote areas, due to the ignorance and superstition of ghosts and gods among the people in the city. The notice will be posted on all major roads. The original text is recorded as follows: "It is strictly forbidden to kill sick infants and damage children's corpses. However, recent investigations have found that there are still cases of cut infant corpses in remote areas. After repeated investigations, it has been found that most of them are ignorant people who superstitiously believe in ghosts and gods and have the saying of repeatedly injuring children or chopping sick or dead children to ward off evil stars. This is extremely cruel and inhuman, and also violates the criminal law. Killing a sick child constitutes the crime of murder and shall be punished with death or life imprisonment according to law. Chopping a child's corpse constitutes the crime of damaging a corpse and shall be punished with imprisonment for a term of not less than six months and not more than five years. Ignorant people, lightly believing in unfounded rumors, have violated the law and are extremely pitiable. This notice is specially reissued to reiterate the prohibition, and I hope that you will not deliberately violate the prohibition and test the law. This is a serious matter."

Bloodshed at Tianyun Building

Female Tea Server Stabbed Three Times

Wang Futin's Brutal Nature

Ms. Wu Yang, known as Sanmei, a female server at the Tianyun Building amusement hall of Wing On Company, formed an intimate relationship with Wang Futin from Shaoxing in February of this year. They rented a house together in Zhabei. Wang, being over the age of discretion and having a coarse temperament, had no stable occupation and associated with idlers. However, Yang Sanmei held a different view and favored him, willingly entering into a cohabitation. She provided for him, but after three months, she regretted her initial choice, leading to frequent conflicts. By April 28th, they separated. But Wang harbored resentment. On the first of this month, at 7:30 PM, Wang purchased a sharp butcher knife and went to Tianyun Building. Upon meeting Sanmei, he lured her outside with a pretext. Sanmei, remembering their past affection, could not refuse. As they walked together, while on the staircase between the fourth and third floors, Wang suddenly pulled out the butcher knife from his sleeve and repeatedly slashed Sanmei's neck three times. Sanmei cried out in pain and fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Wang abandoned the knife and fled, but was apprehended by Huang Shouan, who was ascending the stairs, and handed over to the No. 45 Indian police officer, along with the murder weapon. The injured woman was taken to the Laozha Police Station. After questioning, the police dispatched detectives to send Yang Sanmei to Renji Hospital for treatment. Wang Futin was taken to the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning, where Judge Qian interrogated him. Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang charged him with attempted murder under Article 282 of the Criminal Code. However, due to the victim being still in the hospital, he requested the case be postponed for further questioning. The defendant admitted that after leaving Ningbo, he sent three letters to Wu Yangmei, but received no response. He returned to Shanghai on October 30th and purchased the knife from a Japanese store in the Hongkou Triangle Market. He also confessed to slashing the woman's neck three times at Tianyun Building. He claimed that he had no intention of killing her, only to scare her. Judge Qian, finding the defendant's brutality and claim of merely scaring her to be a blatant attempt to shirk responsibility, ordered him to be detained and the case adjourned for seven days, pending the victim's recovery.

Peng Zhaoliang Reports to Police

Repeatedly Opening and Liquidating Cigarette Factories

Hong Cangting and Weiting Brothers Accused

Aggrieved Parties File Lawsuit in Anger

The Hong Cangting and Weiting brothers from Ningbo have been involved in the cigarette business in Shanghai for many years. Since the 16th year of the Republic (1927), they have opened numerous cigarette factories or tobacco companies. Each time, they would assume key positions as managers or deputy managers. However, the businesses never lasted long, either closing down completely or changing their brand names, and declaring liquidation. Consequently, each liquidation resulted in considerable losses for those who were owed money and other creditors, while the Hong brothers' pockets were filled through the liquidation process. Chen Jimao, also from Ningbo, was a tobacco leaf merchant. Since the Hong brothers established the Huada Cigarette Factory in early 1927, he traded with them. Each time Hong liquidated a business, Chen suffered losses. On the first of last month, the Hong brothers' Huada Yuanji company declared liquidation again, and Chen's losses from dishonored checks were even greater, which he could no longer tolerate. He hired lawyer Xi Ya'fu to file a criminal self-accusation against Hong Cangting and Weiting for fraudulent acquisition of property. He stated that the defendants opened the Huada Cigarette Factory in 1927, which quickly went bankrupt and declared liquidation. In 1930, they renamed it Huada Shenji and continued operations, only to go bankrupt again. In 1933, they renamed it Huayuan Yuanji. However, after less than a year, on October 1st, they employed the same old trick and declared liquidation. The defendants always seized opportunities to accumulate debt, harming hundreds of merchants. The plaintiff, Chen, traded with the defendants extensively, suffering the most severe losses. Since 1933, he had provided tobacco leaves worth 60,000 dollars, but before the payment was made, the defendants mortgaged the tobacco leaves to the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, using foreign capital to engage in fraudulent business. The checks they issued, totaling $59,192.42, were returned due to insufficient funds. After repeated negotiations, he was able to redeem the tobacco leaves. After selling the leaves and repaying the mortgage, there was a remaining balance of $7,226. Adding the remaining $14,726 from the Huacheng Tobacco Company shares and the amount received from cashing checks, he was still defrauded of $22,505.60. Now, the defendants were again using the guise of liquidation and intended to discount and repay their debts. The fact that the defendants had opened cigarette factories, changed their names multiple times within a few years, and were always managed by the two brothers indicated a hidden agenda. The most obvious aspect was that they could obtain illegal profits by discounting and repaying debts through the name of liquidation. Therefore, their opening of cigarette factories was nothing more than a tool for fraud, violating Article 163 of the Negotiable Instruments Law. Therefore, he filed a self-accusation requesting that they be punished according to the law and ordered to repay the defrauded amount of $22,505.60. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng of the First District Local Court held a hearing. The defendants also hired lawyer Wang Zijian to defend them. Judge Huang, noting that the parties were initially friends, ordered them to attempt to reconcile outside of court. The case was adjourned for further hearing. When Hong's cigarette factory declared liquidation last year, it was also accused of fraud in court by a customer because the foreign checks they paid were worthless and the goods had been secretly mortgaged in advance. This is the second time they have been accused.

Bordering the river and the sea, it boasts natural beauty, fresh air, and convenient transportation. A visit to the garden is sure to refresh the mind and spirit, making it a scenic spot in Shanghai.

Central Chemical Glass Factory招待es Reporters for a Tour Yesterday

Yesterday afternoon, the Central Chemical Glass Factory on Pingliang Road招待ed reporters at Yizhixiang on Simadu Road. Over thirty reporters attended. Manager Qian Xinzhi gave a speech, followed by a speech by Guan Guanzhi, a chemistry professor at Datong University. After the meal, they toured the factory. Here is a brief account of the event:

General Remarks

Our country has been learning from the West for several decades, but due to years of war, the results have not been satisfactory. Therefore, science and culture are still lagging behind. Recently, with deepening pain, Chinese scholars know that only by promoting science can China be saved. Therefore, we are promoting scientific research on one hand and striving to popularize scientific knowledge on the other. This is truly a good phenomenon in our country, and we are extremely gratified. However, the instruments, reagents, and other items used in scientific research must all be imported from abroad. Glassware and reagents are especially expensive. Not only is it time-consuming to order, but the price is also extremely high. This often prevents many schools, hospitals, and scholars from acquiring complete equipment due to economic constraints. This greatly hinders the freedom of scientific and cultural progress in our country. In view of this, with the aim of "Every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the nation," we have raised funds and built a factory to specialize in the production of various chemical and medical glassware, as well as modern household glassware. We have hired contemporary experts to carefully review each product, ensuring that the products are exquisite and the prices are very low, to serve the whole country and promote the popularization of science and culture. Retrieving foreign exchange outflow is a secondary matter. We hope that the press will promote our efforts. We would be most grateful.

Product Types

(1) Ordinary chemical glassware, including beakers, flasks, evaporating dishes, glass covers, funnels, retort stands, condensers, gas generators, gas dryers, distillation and evaporation apparatus, desiccators, gas scrubbers, gas absorbers, glass mirrors, glass tubes, alcohol lamps, etc. (2) Quantitative analysis glassware, including graduated cylinders, pipettes, volumetric flasks, graduated cylinders, beakers, weighing devices.

Tour Sequence

(Furnace Room) The glass factory is similar to ordinary factories in that all products must be made in the furnace room. Therefore, the first step is for the engineer to mix the various raw materials and load them into boxes. These are then added to the furnace at the appropriate time and burned for more than ten hours, stirred continuously to melt them evenly. Then, the molten material is scooped out with iron or glass tubes, placed in iron molds to form the desired shape, and sent to the annealing oven. The temperature is gradually reduced over more than 24 hours before being removed. (Machine Room) Processing includes cutting, grinding, baking, engraving, etc. Another part is sent separately. (Natural Fire Room) Processing involves bending the tubes into shape. The reporters deeply praised these processes. The factory also prepared dozens of gifts to be distributed to the attendees.

Hu Minggao, Impersonating a Lawyer, Receives a Reduced Sentence of Six Months

Hu Minggao from Qidong was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for fraudulently using the lawyer's certificate of Wu Zhifen from Anhui to join the Shanghai Bar Association and practice law in Shanghai. This was discovered through a secret report and investigated by the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office. Hu appealed to the Jiangsu High Court for a third instance. The sentence from the first instance was then appealed for. The Jiangsu High Court has now issued a verdict which has now been handed down. The main points of the verdict of the Jiangsu High Court are excerpted below. Regarding the case of Hu Minggao impersonating lawyer Wu Zhifen, the main text of the verdict is that the original verdict and the verdict of the first instance are revoked. The sentence is changed to six months of imprisonment. The diplomas from the Minguo College of Political Science and Law, the lawyer's certificate from the former Beijing government, the lawyer's certificate from the Judicial Administration Department of the National Government, the membership certificate from the Shanghai Bar Association, and the payment receipts are all confiscated.

Dispute over the Sale of Samsung Properties

Zhou Bingcheng and Pang Zhongchen Accused

Zhou Bingcheng, manager of the Samsung Theater, and Pang Laichen (residing at 563 World Lane, Chengdu Road, Beijing Road), owner of the Rongzhang Paper Mill in Nanxun, have been accused of criminal embezzlement and breach of trust by Li Zhongxiang, owner of Fuchangxin Lime Store on Guangxi Road, and Zhang Shenru. They have hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Court. The reasons for the lawsuit are that the property of the Samsung Real Estate Company, recently managed by Zhou Bingcheng, was jointly organized by the late Huang Chu Jiu, Zhao Ruquan, and Zhou Bingcheng. Therefore, all the assets of the company were jointly owned by the Huang family. Since Huang's death, it was agreed that the assets would be liquidated. All of Huang's assets were submitted to the Second Special District Court for execution. Therefore, Huang's property could not be disposed of by anyone without the court's disposition or the consent of all creditors. It has come to light that Zhou Bingcheng sold the Samsung company to Pang Laichen for 300,000 dollars, privately embezzling and dividing the profits, harming the interests of the plaintiffs. This violated Articles 357 and 367 of the Criminal Code. Therefore, the plaintiffs, as creditors of the company, request that the case be investigated and prosecuted according to the law, and additionally file a civil lawsuit requesting compensation for all damages incurred and confirmation that the sales transaction is invalid. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng summoned both defendants. Both defendants appeared. The plaintiffs Li Zhongxiang and others submitted their cases and detailed the above circumstances. When questioned, Zhou Bingcheng stated that the sale of the company was with the consent of Zhao Ruquan and the Huang family and sold to Pang Laichen for 270,000 dollars. Pang admitted to purchasing the company, claiming ignorance of the fact that Huang's property was included. Testimony at the court stated that the company was liquidated by accountant Pan Zhaobang. Therefore, the judge adjourned the case to investigate with accountant Pan before further verification.

###戴春林被控冒牌案判決無罪

The Dai Chunlin Dingji Perfume Shop on Fangbang Road in this city, which produces small boxes of rouge with the "Flying Energy" trademark, was once sued by the Xinhua Industrial Society because the trademark was similar to the "Flying Horse" trademark produced by the Xinhua Industrial Society. However, someone came forward to mediate, and the case was withdrawn. In August of this year, the court returned all the seized goods. In June of this year, Dai Chunlin changed to a new design, using a flower pot as a trademark, and applied to the Trademark Bureau for registration in accordance with Article 37, Paragraph 3 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Trademark Law. Subsequently, on July 23, the Trademark Bureau issued an approval, approving the rejection of Dai Chunlin's continued application for review. The manager of Xinhua Industrial Society, Zha Zixiu, then sued Dai Chunlin for infringing on the trademark and requested investigation. Prosecutor Li Fen's investigation found that Cao Yinmei, the manager of the store, had committed a crime under Article 268 of the Criminal Law, and a public prosecution was initiated. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Qianchang publicly tried the case in the Ninth Court. The defendant, Wei Yinmei, hired lawyer Wang Jian to appear in court to defend him. As a result, the court announced the verdict, acquitting the defendant.

Country Woman Meets Swindler on the Road, Deceived into Sex and Defrauded of Money, Apprehended and Requesting Investigation

Jiang the Monk Seduced Chen Gu Shi

Chen Gu Shi from Jingjiang, 28 years old, came to Shanghai from the countryside this autumn in July to look for her husband, Chen Yifei (from Chongming), but failed to find him. She then temporarily resided with relatives who ran a teahouse at No. 7 Guyuefang, Hongqiao Road, West Shanghai. On the morning of August 2nd, Chen Gu Shi walked to the alley entrance of Jiaotong University, intending to take the No. 2 tram to Shanghai to look for her husband. She happened to meet Jiang the Monk, a tea customer who frequented the Guyuefang teahouse, also waiting for the tram. He asked Chen Gu Shi where she was going, and she truthfully told him. Jiang, seeing that the country woman was easy to deceive, said, "I know Chen Yifei. I met him a few days ago somewhere. He is now a partner in a shop. I will take you there." She believed him and got off the bus at the Eight Immortals Bridge. He deceived her into a certain inn and forcibly raped her. The next morning, he also swindled her gold ring and 30 yuan in cash. After waiting for a long time without him returning, she went back to her relatives' place in Guyuefang. At the end of August, she took a boat back to her hometown. At the beginning of last month, Gu Shi received a letter from her husband, and she came to Shanghai for the second time, now living at No. 40 Maiqi Lane, Maiqi Road, French Concession. At around 10:00 AM yesterday, Jiang the Monk was walking in Xujiahui when he was spotted by her. She apprehended him and sent him to the police station at the third outpost, where officer Zhang Junlin took him back to the station. Chen Yifei also rushed over after receiving a letter. After questioning by Chief Hong, Chen Yifei and Chen Gu Shi recounted the previous events. When questioned, the defendant Jiang the Monk, 39 years old, residing at No. 2 Youxiang Lane, Hongqiao Road, consistently denied the charges of seduction, rape, and fraud. The chief, noting the conflicting testimonies, ordered that the original plaintiff and the three defendants be sent to the bureau together with written statements for further investigation.

Special Feature

The Land and Population of the Northeast

— Zhang Zisheng

—In Response to Mr. Fang Qiuwei's Review of the Shen Bao Yearbook—

Mr. Fang Qiuwei, in a recently published article in "The Future Magazine" reviewing the Shen Bao Yearbook, stated in the preamble that it was "A Question to Zhang Qiyun Regarding the Status of the Northeast in China." Although I am the editor-in-chief of the Shen Bao Yearbook, I could have avoided answering criticisms directed specifically at the author. However, under the title of Mr. Zhang Qiyun's article, I noted that "...original recorded figures that conflict with the latest investigations by the company will be adjusted appropriately," and the figures regarding the land and population of the Northeast were precisely those that I adjusted and carefully checked; therefore, the "especially the errors in the land and population of the Northeast" mentioned by Mr. Fang in relation to that article should be my responsibility to answer – the entire question will of course be answered by Mr. Zhang Qiyun.

1. Area of Land in Northeast China

In Mr. Zhang Qiyun's original manuscript, the figure for the land area of ​​the Northeast was "using miles as the unit and there was another number. Because the land area table of Shen Bao Yearbook had been agreed upon with several geographers to adopt the accurate figures calculated by Mr. Zeng Shiying as the standard; in order to unify the whole book, it was changed to "The area of ​​the whole of China is 11,173,558 square kilometers, and the area of ​​the four northeastern provinces is 1,285,075 square kilometers." Before Mr. Zeng's "Table of Areas of Provinces and Regions of the Country" has been revised, I cannot admit that the land area figures of the four northeastern provinces in the China Report Yearbook are "a big mistake." Since Mr. Fang has misread the national figures and the figures for the four northeastern provinces which are printed tomorrow in the book, and has also misused the Hua Fang Li figures reported by the Civil Affairs Office of the four provinces in the "Northeast Yearbook" for comparison, it is inevitable that he will feel "the difference is huge, and it cannot be measured in Daoli". Readers who read carefully, if they read the words in the article at the beginning of the 23rd Shen Bao Yearbook and pay attention to the conversion between Gong Fang Li and Hua Fang Li, they will naturally know the answer to the question of "how big is the land of the Northeast".

2. Population of Northeast China

Regarding the population of the four northeastern provinces, the population compilation of the first Shen Bao Yearbook (1933 edition) adopted the figures from the Northeast Yearbook and the Asia New Geography Society; the second (1934 edition) used the report of the overseas consuls in September 1933 - a total of 30,092,900 people - see page 169 of the 1934 Shen Bao Yearbook. I initially wanted to change Mr. Zhang Qiyun's original manuscript of 35 million people, but later, due to the calculation of percentage values, I sent a letter to discuss it. Mr. Zhang replied based on the text on pages 6 to 9 of his book "The Economic Overview of Lost Land in the Northeast", thinking that there was no need to change it. I read the book carefully. I felt that this number also had its own basis, so I kept it as it was. The various statistical figures cited in Mr. Fang's article are mostly used as materials when discussing the population of the Northeast in the book; and they have been published in both Shen Bao Yearbooks. The reason why I did not modify Mr. Zhang Qiyun's figures was the result of reading the book "Economic Overview of Lost Land in the Northeast"; at first, like Mr. Fang, I intuitively thought that the figures "would undoubtedly be wrong."

3. Shen Bao Yearbook Welcomes Criticism

Although I have explained the two points criticized by Mr. Fang above; I am very impressed by Mr. Fang's enthusiasm for hoping to improve the Shen Bao Yearbook. - Criticism is the mirror of the editor. The Shen Bao Yearbook is gradually moving towards precision. It needs the guidance of critics, and it needs concrete and practical instructions in the criticism.

As Mr. Fang said in the "Introduction to the Shen Bao Yearbook" in the World Daily on May 22, "Editing a yearbook is the most difficult thing." Although the colleagues of the Shen Bao Yearbook Society have done their best to work hard for two years, and sought help everywhere, after the completion of the two books, after the critics' instructions and their own review, they inevitably discovered some defects and errors. I know that it is necessary to obtain the assistance of experts and scholars from all over the country in order to compile a general yearbook that can satisfy people in China where various accurate materials are not easy to obtain. Now the third Shen Bao Yearbook is being revised, and I hope that those who cherish their reputation will not hesitate to provide materials in the active aspect to enrich the content. In the passive aspect, please send realistic critical texts for reference in the revision.

Special Issue for the 10th Anniversary of Great China University

— Inscription by Wang Boqun

Publisher's Note

— Wang Boqun

As the saying goes: "Born in sorrow, die in ease." The life of an individual is like this, and so is the life of a group. Our Great China was born in June of the 13th year of the Republic of China. Initially, more than 300 students from Xiamen University, due to improper measures by the authorities that could not be salvaged, left the school together and came to Shanghai, requesting former Xiamen University professors Ou Yuanhuai, Wang Yuxiang, Chuan Shishuo, and others to establish a new school for them to continue their studies. And the professors were all able to shoulder the responsibility without hesitation, and based on the original intention of cooperation between teachers and students, they began to prepare for the new school, and named it Great China University, to commemorate the source of the school's history; is this spirit of struggle and sacrifice not commendable? However, at the beginning of the opening, the economic fundraising was very difficult, so all facilities were simple and crude, and the traces were unbearable. At that time, there were only more than 200 students; the school building on Xiaoshadu Road rented three floors above ground and three floors below ground, and all classrooms, offices, and laboratories were in it. The narrow situation was almost impossible to describe! However, the teachers and students of our Great China were able to move forward with the spirit of hard work, hard teaching, and hard study, and persevered. As of today, the school's progress is advancing by leaps and bounds. On the banks of Fanwangdu, thousands of acres of land are wide, and towering buildings are stacked up, and the atmosphere is new. The total number of faculty, staff, and students exceeds 2,000. The graduates who have served the society have been able to constantly improve themselves and have outstanding performance. All of this is the result of ten years of struggle in sorrow and hardship, and it is what we can be proud of.

Although university education is a matter of great importance. Our Great China has taken the task of glorifying China as its own responsibility, and the mission it bears is even more grand! If we do not establish a central goal, we will be building a car behind closed doors and will inevitably not be able to fit the track. Since the opening of the sea ban, the European and American imperialists have competed to bring their material civilization forces deep into China. They occupied our land, infringed on our sovereignty, exploited our people, and squeezed our economy; at the same time, they colluded with domestic soldiers to cause endless internal strife and disturbance. Eventually, they trapped our nation in the ranks of semi-colonies! At this time, when foreign insults are coming and the country is dying, if we do not awaken national consciousness and promote national spirit, how can we revive and abolish the decline? The university is the highest academic research institution, and if we continue to be complacent and step on the old ways, what good will it do to the current difficulties! This school examines the world's trends externally and observes the social environment internally, and deeply feels that university education in China at the current stage should take the restoration of the nation as its highest origin. Under this principle, the direction of our efforts can be divided into four: (1) Vigorously implement personality education to cultivate sound national morality. (2) Promote production education to rescue the dying national economy. (3) Encourage science education to develop the infinite natural treasures. (4) Implement national defense education to cultivate the nation's ability to defend itself. If we can stick to this goal and carry it through to the end, then the national self-confidence will be established, and the material construction force will gradually be enriched, and then the life of the entire nation can get rid of the shackles of imperialists and stand upright in the world of survival of the fittest. The meaning of this school's implementation of the education of restoring the nation lies in this.

Today is the 10th anniversary of this school. All teachers and students of the school, recall the hardships of the creation in those years, silently observe the greatness of the future mission. In addition to issuing special issues by the school's Great China Journal and Weekly Journal to commemorate the celebration, we also publish a commemorative special issue in various newspapers, listing the school's past historical development and future improvement plans, to inform the people of the country and to encourage ourselves. We are grateful for the titles or contributions from Chairman Lin, ministers of various ministries, and school directors, which have enhanced the content. We hope that all teachers and students will carry through the spirit of hard work, hard teaching, and hard study as always, recognize the current crisis of the nation, country, and society, and promote self-improvement and perseverance! At the same time, we also hope that domestic sages and heroes will continue to give instructions and support to our 10-year-old Great China child, so that it can realize the mission of saving the country and glorifying China. It is the fortune of my Great China, and it is also the fortune of the future of the nation and the country.

Great China University's 10th Anniversary of Educating Talents

— Lin Sen

Great China University's 10th Anniversary, Glorifying My China

— Wang Zhaoming

The Formation of a New School Spirit at Great China University

— He Yingqin

Recently, we often hear a disappointing cry, saying that China's school education is going bankrupt. This sentence sounds rather exaggerated at first; but if we savor the facts and achievements of school education in the past few years, we feel that it is reasonable. A part of our Chinese school spirit is really too bad, and this bad school spirit is getting worse day by day. This part of the bad school spirit was mostly formed gradually after the May Fourth Movement. The May Fourth Movement was a movement of national awakening, and it was a glorious product of the young students at that time. But at that time, the youth only had ideals, and there was no basis for the ideals. They pursued the new and enthusiastically admired the new culture of the West, but forgot that the new culture was produced in the old culture, and discarded everything in our Chinese culture. In this almost blind enthusiasm, they only absorbed the dross of the new Western culture. Human nature is easy to be evil and difficult to be good. Young people acted arbitrarily, and the school spirit became more and more arrogant, while the management of the schools became more and more relaxed. In recent years, many young people in schools spend their days there seeking happiness, and they simply don't know what it means to study knowledge and cultivate morality; some even shout slogans there, put up slogans, and are willing to be used by one or two unscrupulous elements in the education or political circles as soldiers for strikes and disturbances. The deterioration of the school spirit is too much.

Great China University's 10th Anniversary Planting Trees and Cultivating Talents

— Wu Jing Wish

Our Great China University has struggled and succeeded in the midst of hardship. Our purpose of establishing the school was to promote the movement of writing books. For the past ten years, the staff has worked hard, the teachers have taught hard, and the students have studied hard. A school spirit of simplicity, hard work, and hard study has long been cultivated. In October last year, it was decided to take national revival as the general goal of university education in the future, and listing the promotion of our country's inherent culture as the first step in the implementation outline. This kind of radical and forgetful youth mentality left over from the May Fourth Movement can be swept away. However, in the period of unprecedented national crisis, if we want to revive the nation, we must list several concrete goals and further cultivate our new school spirit in a practical way. In this way, we can shoulder the difficulties of the times and promote the Great China's spirit of establishing the school.

1. Cultivate the spirit of sacrifice for the country and the nation

The weakness of our country is due to the fact that the majority of the people are too selfish and self-interested, and lack the concept of a nation and a country. All that is beneficial to the individual is sought at the expense of everything; if it is only beneficial to the nation and the country but not to the individual, then not only is it indifferent, but even tries to sabotage it in various ways. Our Great China University was created from the spirit of sacrifice. From now on, this spirit of sacrifice should be extended to the national and national aspects. We must make young students get rid of the inferior root of selfishness and self-interest, stimulate their love for the nation and the country, only know the great self of 400 million people united in sincerity, and not know the insignificant small self; if we encounter national crisis, everyone should have the determination to sacrifice the small self and save the great self.

2. Strictly make teachers and students take responsibility

It is a matter of course that teachers are responsible for guiding and teaching, and students are responsible for diligent study. However, in some schools, teachers only seek to get by and perfunctorily do things. They listen to the bell, go to class, and leave class. They even try to please students in order to secure their jobs. Some think that being a teacher is a last resort. Students mostly aim to exchange diplomas for qualifications. They are unwilling to study and are only arrogant, lazy, extravagant, and form factions to create evil. The wind of hard teaching and hard study at our Great China University has been deeply ingrained. From now on, we should carefully select teachers who can take responsibility thoroughly, and should not use qualifications as the standard; the students' homework and morality should be managed absolutely strictly. We must know that the student era is definitely not an era of freedom. In the current serious national crisis, none of us has personal freedom, especially students should not be free. The students of our Great China should automatically take the responsibility of students and exchange freedom for the price of work.

Great China University's 10th Anniversary Commemoration of the Civilization of Great China, October 1934

— Dai Chuanxian respectfully congratulates

3. Find ways to make the relationship between teachers and students closer

In most schools, teachers and students form two non-communicating barriers. Teachers teach for a year, but they still don't recognize the names of a few students; students listen to a year of classes, but they have never talked to a teacher once. As a result, the efficiency of teachers' teaching and the benefits of students' study are limited to a few short hours. After class, the relationship between teachers and students is over. This kind of separation can also make students feel that learning is boring and monotonous, and thus perfunctory and lazy. The banner of our Great China University was originally cooperation between teachers and students; the tutor system, which is now popular all over the country, was first advocated by our Great China University. From now on, we should strengthen cooperation and promote the tutor system, so that the feelings and thoughts of both teachers and students can be further closer, teachers can give sincere guidance, and students can accept it sincerely.

4. Pay attention to popularizing physical education and military training

Chinese people have always been unconcerned about physical health, so there is a joke about the sick men of East Asia. Scholars even believe that being weak is the true color of a scholar. Now we have realized the importance of physical health, and we should focus on hygiene and exercise. However, physical education courses in schools are mostly equal to a formality. Even if there are a few schools famous for physical education, they only take competitive martial arts as the whole of physical education, and cultivating athletes is the only purpose. As for military training, it is even more of a formal affair, and even pampered soldiers cannot be trained. Our Great China University has implemented popular physical education since this semester, and pays special attention to the actual military life in military training. From now on, we should mobilize all students to carry out strict and disciplined training, so that every student has a healthy physique, a lively spirit, a habit of hard work, and a style of observing the law.

5. Make students' lives adapt to social life

The gap between school and society is one of the biggest shortcomings of education in our country. The purpose of education is to create people who can be self-reliant and useful to society; if school and society are two completely different stages, how can a young person who comes out of school suddenly jump into society and apply himself? Many schools now are manufacturing the following two types of people: the first type is dreamers, who hold overly grand ideals, and have absolutely insufficient understanding and cultivation of the actual society; the second type is high-level vagrants, who don't even have the ability to daydream, They only care about eating well, dressing fashionably, and living comfortably. Outside of school, they go to tea houses and restaurants, and even go to dance halls to dance. They are ignorantly unaware that there is a completely different big society outside the school gate - in this big society, it is necessary to use great labor to fight for the right to live. We try to imagine that these two types of people, running into society, are not just parasites? Now the outcry of "graduation is unemployment" is rampant, but in fact, the most important reason for this "graduation is unemployment" is that the school has failed to train talents who can adapt to society. "Unable to reach the high, unable to reach the low," only shouting about unemployment. Our Great China University has long established a public education experimental zone to enable students to go to the countryside to serve. From now on, we should further make students' lives farmerized and adapt to the actual social life.

All the teachers and students of our Great China University! We should have great awareness and determination, take the nation and the country as the premise in everything, sacrifice personal freedom, and seek the freedom of the majority; and on the basis of our inherent culture and virtues, seek new development and creation. Our national spirit of hard work, the old virtues of filial piety, loyalty, trust, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the foundation of our Chinese nation's founding, and the reason why our Chinese nation has created a glorious history of four thousand years. We should follow the broad road taken by our ancestors and march forward with courage and self-confidence! At the same time, we should also carry through the spirit of establishing our Great China University, bury our heads in hard work, bury our heads in hard teaching, bury our heads in hard study, create a new school spirit, and prepare for the world's great unity by working hard day and night.

Great China University's 10th Anniversary, For the Sake of Opening the World to Peace

— Yu Youren

大夏 University and National Revival Education

— Wu Tiecheng

Da Xia University was founded in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China and has already passed through ten years. President Wang Yu-Gong is one of the school's directors and has sent a letter soliciting articles to commemorate the anniversary. I believe that Da Xia has, in its short ten-year history, progressed from a newly established school with pioneering spirit to one that is competing with other famous universities in the country. Its remarkable and splendid development deserves to be celebrated. Furthermore, at this critical juncture of national peril and cultural decline, Da Xia deeply feels the importance of its mission to cultivate talent for the country and upholds its consistent principle of saving the nation through education. Starting from last autumn, it has designated national revival as the central goal of education. This matter concerns the future of the country and the nation, and it is of utmost importance and significance. Therefore, it is necessary to explore it in detail. I am writing this article with the hope of discussing it with my fellow countrymen.

In the international arena of the 20th century, there is a dazzling phenomenon that leads to prosperity if followed, and ruin if defied, which is the development of national culture. Culture is the life force and expression of survival struggle of a nation. In terms of its "essence," it is the sum total of material and spiritual achievements of a nation in its efforts to cope with the environment, improve society, and strive for progress. In terms of its "function," it is a vital element for any nation seeking survival, prosperity, and development, which cannot be dispensed with even for a moment. Looking back at history and observing the changes in the world, the rise and fall, strength and weakness, and superiority and inferiority of all nations are all attributed to the prosperity or decline of their culture.

Our Chinese nation resides in the Asian continent and has been a nation of propriety and culture since ancient times, with a long and glorious history. Although it has been ravaged by foreign tribes several times, it has been able to maintain its great power without being assimilated. On the contrary, all foreign tribes that invaded our country were eventually assimilated by us. This is because the excellent culture of our Chinese nation made it possible. Examining the culture of the Chinese nation, in terms of spirit, it is "extremely great and strong, supremely impartial and upright," "intelligent and wise, sufficient to oversee; generous and gentle, sufficient to accommodate; vigorous and resolute, sufficient to execute; orderly and righteous, sufficient to command respect; cultured and meticulous, sufficient to distinguish." Therefore, it can traverse tens of thousands of miles and span thousands of years, exerting its innate intelligence to cope with complex environments, rectify the mind, cultivate the self, investigate things, and extend knowledge. As for material civilization, when the world was still in its infancy, in a state of primordial chaos, with people behaving like beasts, we had You Chao Shi teaching the people to build houses, Sui Ren Shi teaching the people to cook with fire, Fu Xi Shi teaching the people to fish and hunt with nets, Shen Nong Shi teaching the people to cultivate and plant crops, Huang Di creating boats and vehicles and building palaces, and Xia Yu controlling floods and benefiting the people's livelihood. Thus, they initiated the evolution of our country's society and elevated the common people. What is particularly worthy of boasting to the world is that the invention of printing, gunpowder, and the compass not only preceded ancient cultures but also served as a driving force for the promotion of Western culture when they were introduced to Europe in the Yuan Dynasty. Such examples are too numerous to mention, and these are just the more prominent ones.

Da Xia University Tenth Anniversary Nurturing Talent for the Country

— Sun Ke's Inscription

Unfortunately, since the Han Dynasty, scholars have advocated conservatism and rejected progress, focusing on textual criticism and sentence analysis. During the Jin and Wei Dynasties, and the Six Dynasties, the trend of Huang-Lao Daoism and empty talk was promoted, creating an extremely romantic and decadent nature. Later, the Tang Dynasty valued commentaries and sub-commentaries, the Song Dynasty valued metaphysics, the Ming Dynasty valued stereotyped essays, and the Qing Dynasty valued textual research. The thoughts of various schools were suppressed, and the pursuit of knowledge through investigation was despised. As a result, the inherent ability of our nation to create culture completely disappeared, and the scientific and artistic lifestyle, as well as the ability to organize the country and govern society, all declined. In modern times, metaphysical discussion and humor have become increasingly empty. Corruption and decadence have made the people's aspirations increasingly humble. They do not know how to conserve, nor can they create. The whole country is in a state of panic, feeling hopeless about the future, passively shrinking, and creating a society of complicity. The reasons for this are complex and diverse, but they are mainly due to the weakening of national self-confidence and material creativity. Today, in order to correct these malpractices and revive the nation-state, there is a cultural revival movement. The so-called cultural revival movement aims to enhance the self-confidence and creativity of our Chinese nation, recognize the glorious history of the nation in the past, to promote and amplify the excellent culture we share. At the same time, we should grasp the current stage of international turmoil, fierce competition for survival, and strive to study material science to meet the needs of time and space and seek adaptation. We should also build a new cultural system to complete the great mission of national revival.

Da Xia University Tenth Anniversary A Heavy Responsibility and a Long Road Ahead

— Wang Shijie's Inscription

The path to reviving the nation and building culture is certainly not limited to one aspect. The creation of culture, the preservation of national essence, the enlightenment of wisdom, the strengthening of physique, the cultivation of personality, and the promotion of national spirit all rely on education as the key to creation. University education, in particular, as the highest institution for cultivating talents and researching academics, has the mission of nurturing ideas, developing culture, and enabling the Chinese nation to adapt to time and space and continue to survive. At this time of national revival movement, how should the facilities of university education be determined in the future, so that we can relieve the national crisis and make great contributions to overcoming the difficulties of the times? This is what we should deeply understand and study. Now, let's discuss it:

1. Cultivate the Spirit of Creation

Our Chinese nation was rich in the spirit of creating culture thousands of years ago, as has been said before. However, since the implementation of new education, we have been engaged in imitation, taking the imitation of others as an honor. Little do we know that the culture of a nation depends on its own creation and construction, and we cannot take the ready-made things of others for our own use. In the future, the scientific research of university education should analyze the inherent culture of the nation, understand its characteristics and shortcomings, and, based on the needs of modern society, make a precise evaluation of the essential values, and then create a unique culture of our Chinese nation. How to improve living methods, how to determine social organization, how to promote cultural development, and how to engage in national construction should all be based on local teaching materials as the original material and the current situation of China as the object. In this way, the culture of the national heritage and the academic knowledge of social public tools can be promoted and improved, scientific construction can be achieved, and national revival will not be in vain.

2. Cultivate Scientific Skills

The goal of university education is to train specialized skills and improve real life, not just to be a tool for personal fame and gain. However, our nation has been bound by thousands of years of traditional thought, and the focus of education has always been on the cultivation of the spirit, with little emphasis on the art of benefiting the people's livelihood. Since the implementation of new education, this concept is still popular. School curriculum and equipment are mostly contrary to actual life. Students only know how to memorize books, without any real knowledge and practical skills. Therefore, they often lose their jobs in society once they graduate from school. In the future, the facilities of university education should pay more attention to the training of scientific skills. Instead of lecturing on empty theories, it is better to respond to actual needs. Instead of singing high-sounding tunes, it is better to conduct appropriate experiments. We must make the lives of young students reverse the morbid state of the past and conform to the principles of diligence and operation, using both hands and brains, and unifying knowledge and action. In this way, the skills of the profession are prepared, the guarantee of life is naturally solid, and the foundation of the country and society can be stabilized day by day, and the development of agriculture, industry, and commerce can be gradually developed.

Da Xia Tenth Anniversary United Efforts Make a Strong Fortress

— Respectfully Inscribed by He Yingqin

3. Study National Defense Construction

The situation in the Pacific is becoming increasingly urgent, and the global economic turmoil is becoming more intense. Once war breaks out, our "sick man of East Asia" will inevitably bear the brunt. If we do not prepare for the future and pay attention to national defense construction, how can we achieve independence and survive? National defense construction has a broad meaning. Specifically, in the present, it should be about how to revitalize industry and increase production. In the near future, it should be about how to enrich military science and recover lost land. In the distant future, it should be about how to open up the frontier and realize the status of the master of the Pacific. This work, on the one hand, must rely on the government's overall planning and control of the national economy and talent. On the other hand, it must rely on the power of education to cultivate national heroes and leaders. Therefore, when it comes to university education today, in addition to striving for the dissemination of ordinary knowledge, the strengthening of physical fitness, and the cultivation of noble personality, we must have a thorough and precise study of military science, national defense policy, and wartime economy, so as to cultivate their quick and skillful skills. At the same time, students should deeply understand the legacy of great figures in history, the glorious deeds of heroes and patriots who struggled for the country, nurture their psychology of independence and self-respect, perseverance, the will to fight against the enemy, and the spirit of dedication. Only then can they be cultivated into talents who serve the country, and not fail the main purpose of education in extraordinary times.

The above three points are the fundamental principles for reviving national education, and the facilities for this education are the basic work for saving the country and the nation, which is not the sole responsibility of Da Xia University. It is hoped that those who are responsible for university education will strive to move forward from the fundamental construction, and consistently pursue this goal from beginning to end. Although we cannot expect immediate results, the future lifeline of the country depends on it!

Historical Development of Da Xia University

— Wang Yuxiang

1. Introduction

Da Xia has been around for ten years. When we think of the difficulties of founding the school ten years ago, the current situation of more than two thousand teachers and students gathering together, and the seriousness of the national crisis in the universe, we feel that Da Xia will bear a great mission in the future. On the occasion of the tenth anniversary of the conference, I would like to give a general review of the development of Da Xia in the past ten years, and share it with the people, and encourage myself.

2. The Process of Founding Da Xia University

A. The Meaning of "June 1st"

In May of the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, there were 300 university students. Because the measures of the authorities were improper, they rose up to seek remedy, but were not listened to. And a part of the faculty and staff, taking advantage of the opportunity, blinded the president and added oppression, and a great wave arose. The students appealed for ten days, and their voices were hoarse. On June 1, the staff of the Construction Department again led the workers to poison the students Jiao Shiqing, Lei Rongpu, Sun Zuojin, etc. All the students, motivated by righteousness, had no choice but to leave the school, fearing that they would lose their studies halfway and deviate from their original aspirations. They elected representatives He Zhongyan, Ni Wenya, Sun Kangzeng, Shi Naizhu and other fourteen people to Shanghai to request former Xiamen University professors Ou Yuanhuai, Wang Yuxiang, Chuan Shishuo, Yu Zelan, Li Shiqiong, Lin Tianlan, Wu Yuteng, Lü Zifang, Zhou Xuezhang and other nine people to prepare for the new school so that they could get a place to study. Therefore, Da Xia will use this sensational June 1st as the founding anniversary from now on. From this, it can be known that

The "June 1st" commemoration actually contains three important meanings: resisting the powerful and sacrificing blood, building a new school for the reading movement, and supporting justice and teacher-student cooperation.

B. The Naming of "Da Xia"

The cause of the Xiamen University student tide was actually caused by the regional resentment of a part of the faculty and staff. The professors who left the school, at the request of the students, prepared for the new school, and borrowed No. 24 Meiren Lane, Beidi'ao Road, Shanghai as the preparation office, and named the new school "Da Xia". On the one hand, it records the origin of the school history, and on the other hand, it implies the meaning of "carrying forward the glory of China". It is said that "If you can be Xia, you must be great." Da Xia University is a great university. In the future, chasing Harvard and competing with Oxford depends on the self-improvement of all our teachers and students.

C. The Organization of the Board of Directors

After the establishment of the new school preparation office, Mr. Wu Shihui often came to discuss school matters. He once said that at the beginning of running a school, the current problem lies in how to enable students to study and graduate, and there is no need to stick to the form of the school. His words were very encouraging, and the colleagues were deeply grateful. Therefore, five departments of Literature, Science, Education, Commerce, and Preparatory were established. After the plan was determined, Wu Zhihui, Wang Jingwei, Zhang Junmai, Wang Boqun, Ye Chucang, Ma Junwu, Shao Lizi and other gentlemen were invited to be the directors of the school to establish the board of directors as the representative of the school. And Mr. Wang Boqun donated 2,000 yuan for start-up expenses. At that time, the situation of struggling to make ends meet is still vivid in my mind.

Ten Years to Grow Trees, A Hundred Years to Nurture People

— Ju Xin

D. The Process of Approving the Record

At the beginning of the school, No. 201 Xiaoshadu Road was rented as a temporary school building. The narrowness of the buildings and the simplicity of the equipment were inevitable. However, the school is a product of the reading movement, and teachers and students can all uphold the "three hardships spirit" - teachers teach hard, staff work hard, and students study hard - and strive for cooperation, so it has won the support of many people in the community. In March of the fourteenth year, the Ministry of Education sent personnel to the school to inspect, and recognized that the school "teachers and management were serious, and the academic style and results were excellent." On July 28 of the same year, the Ministry of Education approved the record for trial operation. In the spring of the eighteenth year, the school purchased more than 300 acres of the new campus site in Fanwangdu, and the material foundation was more solid. On April 6, the Ministry of Education approved the board of directors to register. On April 30, the Ministry of Education sent personnel to the school for inspection again, and was satisfied with all aspects of the school's measures. Therefore, on May 17 of the eighteenth year, it approved the official registration. After that, our school worked harder and became one of the famous universities in the country.

3. Evolution of Administrative Organization

The administrative system of the school has undergone four changes. The first phase was the committee system, the second phase was the president system, the third phase was the committee system again, and the fourth phase was the president system again. At the beginning of the establishment of the school in the thirteenth year, because the directors of the schools were scattered in various places, it was not easy to gather. Therefore, Ou Yuanhuai, Wang Yuxiang, and Chuan Shishuo and other three professors were temporarily appointed as executive secretaries to hire the first phase of teachers. After the school started, the school affairs became more complicated, so Lu Jizeng, Xu Zhang, and Zhang Menglin were added to the school affairs conference to maintain the school affairs. On November 22, the first board of directors was convened, and Dr. Ma Junwu was elected as the president, and Mr. Wang Boqun was elected as the chairman of the board of directors. In January of the sixteenth year, President Ma firmly resigned due to the relationship with Guangxi University. At that time, the National Government promoted the committee system, and the school changed the president system to the committee training, and Mr. Wang Boqun was elected as the chairman of the university committee by the board of directors, and the school affairs administration committee was changed to the university committee, which was organized by ten members. In March of the seventeenth year, in accordance with the school regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education, the committee system was changed to the president system again. Mr. Wang Boqun was elected as the president by the board of directors, and Mr. Ou Yuanhuai was the vice president. At the same time, the university committee was changed to the school affairs conference. Up to now, there has been no change, and the administrative foundation has become more consolidated.

4. Changes in School Buildings

The school buildings have undergone three moves. During the preparation period, it was at No. 24 Meiren Lane, Beidi'ao Road, French Concession, Shanghai.
