At the beginning of the school, No. 201 Xiaoshadu Road was rented as a temporary school building, with three floors and three bottoms, shaped like an ancient temple. All classrooms, offices, laboratories, and libraries were in it. The dormitory was in Zhiheli, Robison Road, and the road in front of the house was used as a basketball court. The author could not name it, and once named it the Jumping Era. In the summer of the fourteenth year, the May 30th Massacre occurred, and British soldiers pressed the border and occupied our school building. The school moved to the Pan Family Ancestral Hall in Binlang Road to work in the two doormen. They also negotiated with the Pan family landlord to borrow land to build a school building, and after several twists and turns, they finally got their wish. In the autumn, they moved to the school building at No. 301 Jiaozhou Road for classes, and rented more than 20 acres of vacant land next to the school as a sports field. Later, the number of students increased sharply, and a dormitory was added on the opposite side of the Jiaozhou Road school building, and two small classrooms were added. A piece of land was rented on the left side of Robison Road to build a girls' dormitory. At this time, the environment was better, because all the houses and land were rented, so it was once named the "Cherish the Light Era". In this "Borrowing Light Era", it has been five years. It was not until Di in the nineteenth year that he moved to the self-built new school building of the "Mansion Era" in Fanwangdu. The scale is magnificent, the school grounds are empty, the air is fresh, and the environment is quiet. It is a paradise for young students to study.

Da Xia University Tenth Anniversary Nurturing People

— Wu Tiecheng

5. Concluding Remarks

The above is only a brief report on the founding process of our Da Xia, the evolution of the administrative organization, and the changes in the school buildings. Other important developments and improvements of various departments will be described in special articles, so I will not repeat them here. But there is an ancient saying: "Worry and labor can prosper the country, and idleness and pleasure can destroy oneself." "People are born in worry and die in happiness." Individuals are like this, countries are like this, and groups are also like this. Remembering the past and looking forward to the future, I feel the danger of the national revival of our country and encourage myself even more. In the winter of the twenty-second year, the outline of national revival education was formulated and implemented, with a period of three years, as the central goal of the efforts of all teachers and students of the school. The Yi Jing says: "Its demise, its demise, is hit by the mulberry." At this time of national crisis, who will be the maintainer of the mulberry? The spirit of struggle, sacrifice, and creation of our Da Xia is not the pearl of our nation's survival.

Da Xia University Tenth Anniversary Special Issue A Grand View

— Inscribed by Chu Minyi

Overview of the Current Situation of Da Xia University

— Chuan Shishuo

1. School Buildings

Since the establishment of the school in June of the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, all the school buildings have been rented until the autumn of the nineteenth year. The situation of trudging is self-evident. In the spring of the eighteenth year, President Wang, in view of the advancement of school affairs and the sharp increase in students, resolutely took the construction of permanent school buildings as his own responsibility. He raised funds one after another to purchase more than 300 acres of school land beside Zhongshan Road in Fanwangdu. On New Year's Day of the nineteenth year, he broke ground and built the first phase of the school building, which was completed in September. There is a large classroom, named Qunxian Hall, which is a three-story steel-concrete building with a flat roof in the shape of a character. The lower floor is the office, and the second and third floors are classrooms, which can accommodate 2,000 students. There are two male dormitories, named Quncezhai and Qunlizhai, which are three-story gray brick buildings in the shape of a concave character, each of which can accommodate 720 students. There is a girls' dormitory, named Qunyingzhai, which can accommodate 400 students. In addition, there is a canteen, a bathroom, a temporary auditorium, and four temporary classrooms and offices. At the end of the year, three faculty and staff dormitories were built, totaling 72 rooms, and a temporary science museum was built. In the summer of the twentieth year, a sanatorium and a temporary library were added. In the summer of the twenty-third year, because the large and middle departments shared the school building, it was inconvenient for teaching and management. Therefore, more than 30 acres of land was allocated to the east of the school river and south of the sports field to build a new school building for the affiliated Da Xia Middle School, including an office hall and two classrooms in the shape of a product. It was completed in the autumn and the class was moved to the upper floor.

2. School Scenery

The school is located beside Zhongshan Road in Fanwangdu, Xihai, Shanghai, covering an area of more than 300 acres. The layout of the school is in the style of a garden. The southernmost is Da Xia New Village, with clear water and weeping willows on both banks. The faculty and staff dormitories are hidden among them. To the north of the village is the girls' dormitory Qunyingzhai, to the east of the hall is the library, and to the north is the forest area. The trees are shaded and the old trunks reach the sky, mixed with countless elm, poplar, peach and willow trees. Crossing the forest area and crossing a small bridge to the north is a large square, which can be 30 acres, with flagpoles erected in the middle, surrounded by shrubs, and the edges are like carpets, which can be used for rest after class. To the north of the square is Qunxian Hall, and to the east and west of the hall are the male dormitories Qunce and Qunli Halls. To the north are the temporary auditorium, science museum, after-school club, bathroom, artesian well machine room, and sanatorium. In front of the hospital is a lotus pond, which can be several acres in size, with lotus leaves and fish playing east and west. It is enough to travel around and enjoy the scenery. From the sanatorium to the school river (that is, Liwa Lida River, donated to the school by Mr. Rong Zongjing), the plains are vast and boundless, which is the large sports field. In the northeast corner of the school river, across a small bridge, is a small island, with winding rivers and clear water that can be seen. The graduates who served the school built a pavilion on it, named "Xia Yu", which can be used for rest. To the south of the sports field is the school building of the affiliated Da Xia Middle School, which is beautiful and magnificent. Looking down at the whole school, there are ancient trees, plains, clear streams, and ponds. There is no noise of the city, and it is rich in natural scenery. It is indeed a good place for young people to study.

The Merit of Promoting National Education: Ten Years and the Limitless Future of Great China University's Tenth Anniversary Special Issue

— Respectfully Inscribed by Pan Zhizhan

3. University Affairs

A. Reorganization of the Board of Trustees: The Board of Trustees of this university was established in the autumn of the thirteenth year [of the Republic], and formally registered in April of the eighteenth year. Last year, in December, it was reorganized in accordance with the revised regulations for private schools promulgated by the Ministry [of Education]. The current list of trustees is as follows:

1. Trustees: Mr. Wang Boqun (Chairman of the Board), Wang Zhixin, Wang Zhiwei, He Yingqin, Jiang Wenyu, Wu Tiecheng, Du Yong, Zhang Zhuping, Yang Yongtai, Chuan Shi Shuo, and Ou Yuanhuai.

2. Honorary Trustees: Mr. Wang Yiting, Wu Zhihui, Wu Yunzhai, Wang Jingwei, Huang Shaoxiong, Ren Jisheng, Shao Lizi, He Zongyan, Zhou Ziliang, Hu Mengjia, Hu Wenhu, Liang Luanan, Xu Xinliu, Xu Jilu, Chen Guangfu, Ma Junwu, Zhang Junqin, Zhang Gongquan, Huang Suchu, Ye Chucang, Rong Zongjing, Yu Qiaqing, Zhao Jinqing, Zhao Hengti, Liu Wenyao, Liu Shufan, Qian Xinzhi, Dai Peiji, and Dai Zengyuan.

B. System of Administrative Organization: The Board of Trustees is the highest authority of the university, and its main functions are to raise university funds and elect the president and vice president, etc. The president is the head of administration and also the chairman of the university affairs meeting. The vice president assists the president in handling university affairs. Under the president, there is a university secretary, a dean of academic affairs, a chief accountant, a chief of general affairs, a dean of student life, deans of various colleges, heads of various departments, a registrar, a librarian, and a director of the affiliated Great China Middle School, one person each. The university affairs meeting is composed of the above-mentioned personnel and three faculty representatives. Under the university affairs meeting, there are six committees: examination, academic affairs, finance, general affairs, library, and student life guidance. The president, dean of academic affairs, chief accountant, chief of general affairs, librarian, and dean of student life serve as ex officio chairmen. Each committee is further divided into groups to handle affairs according to the complexity of its responsibilities, in order to achieve the effect of division of labor and cooperation.

Page 14

C. Departments and Programs of Each College

1. The College of Liberal Arts has three departments: Chinese Studies, English, and History and Sociology.

2. The College of Science has three departments: Mathematics and Physics, Chemistry, and Civil Engineering.

3. The College of Education has three departments: Educational Administration, Educational Psychology, and Social Education.

4. The College of Commerce has four departments: Banking, Accounting, Transportation, and Business Management.

5. The College of Law has three departments: Law, Political Science, and Economics.

6. The Teacher Training Program is divided into four groups: Chinese, English, History and Geography, and Mathematics and Physics.

D. Evaluation of Academic Performance: The university evaluates students' academic performance based on the principle of emphasizing both quality and quantity. The methods are as follows:

1. (Credit): One hour of lecture per week, two hours of self-study, for a full semester constitutes one credit.

2. (Grade): Credits measure quantity, grade points measure quality. Grade points are determined by the grade. If the grade is first class, the grade point is 3; if the grade is second class, the grade point is 2; if the grade is third class, the grade point is 1; fourth-class and fifth-class grades receive no grade points, and fifth-class grades also receive no credits. This is calculated for a one-credit course. The rest can be inferred by analogy.

3. Index: The ratio of credits to grade points is the index. The total grade points for a semester are divided by the total number of credits to obtain the semester's total index. The total grade points earned over four years are divided by the total credits earned to obtain the graduation index.

E. Student ID Number Assignment: Starting this semester, student ID numbers will be assigned. Each student has a student ID number, which will never change once assigned. All registration forms must include the student's ID number for verification and to facilitate teaching.

F. Establishment of Special Lectureships: With the loss of the Northeast and the increasing national crisis, the way to save the nation depends on education. In view of this, the university established various special lectureships in the autumn of the twenty-first year [of the Republic], inviting academic experts from inside and outside the university to give systematic lectures. The lectureships established successively include: 1. Lectureship on Education for National Salvation; 2. Lectureship on National Defense Chemistry; 3. Lectureship on Sino-Japanese Relations; 4. Lectureship on Controlled Economy; 5. Lectureship on Pacific Issues; and the Lectureship on International Issues and the Lectureship on Borderland Issues, which are offered this semester.

G. Expansion of Scholarship Funds

1. University Scholarships: Twenty scholarships per semester, each worth twenty yuan. Students from all colleges and departments who have excellent conduct and an academic index of 2.5 or higher are eligible.

2. Ou Family Scholarship: This spring, Mr. Ou, the vice president of the university, celebrated the seventieth birthday of his respected father, Mr. Jianbo. He generously donated 5,000 yuan from the birthday gifts to establish a scholarship fund for the university. Starting this autumn, the bank will withdraw 500 yuan in interest annually to award scholarships to six students: four university students, each receiving 100 yuan; and two middle school students, each receiving 50 yuan.

3. Private Scholarships: The number of scholarships is not fixed. The criteria for awarding scholarships are specified by the donors and awarded after approval by the university affairs meeting.

4. Special Scholarships: Divided into five categories: Special Topic Research Grants, Speech and Debate Awards, Chinese and English Joint Examination Awards, and All-Around Excellence Awards. The number of scholarships is not fixed and is funded by the fines collected from students who register late each semester.

4. Facilities

A. Library Facilities: The university library currently has a total collection of 32,412 Chinese and Western books and 384 Chinese and Western periodicals. An annual allocation of 10,000 yuan is designated for the purchase of books. The library's reading rooms are divided into seven sections: (1) Reference Reading Room, (2) General Reading Room, (3) Periodical Reading Room, (4) Newspaper Reading Room, (5) Faculty Reading Room, (6) Educational Research Room, and (7) Middle School Collection.

B. Science Facilities

1. Physics Facilities: There are three rooms for the general physics laboratory and storage. There are more than 600 types of measurement instruments, optical instruments, mechanical instruments, thermal instruments, and musical instruments.

2. Chemistry Facilities: There are four laboratories for general chemistry, analytical chemistry, organic chemistry, and industrial chemistry, which can accommodate more than 260 students. In addition, there are three rooms for balances, air, gas, and storage. There are more than 1,780 pounds of inorganic and organic acids, salts, and bases; more than 12,890 pieces of various glassware; more than 580 pieces of automatic distilled water apparatus, high and low-temperature electric furnaces, melting furnaces, thermometers, and hydrometers; and more than 1,200 specimens and charts.

3. Biology Facilities: There are one laboratory, one specimen room, and one storage room. There are 40 microscopes, more than 400 human body models, more than 800 animal specimens, and more than 650 pieces of glassware.

4. Psychology Facilities: There is one laboratory that can accommodate 60 students. There are 32 instruments and 130 charts for experimental psychology.

5. Civil Engineering Facilities: There is one storage room with more than 30 pieces of equipment, including transits, levels, measuring tapes, and level rods. Each survey can be used by 16 people.

C. Physical Education Facilities: The men's sports field is located on the west side of the campus, covering an area of more than 50 mu. It has six tennis courts, four basketball courts, and one soccer field. The soccer field is surrounded by a 400-meter running track, which can accommodate eight people running side by side. Outside the track, there are horizontal bars and other sports equipment and field event facilities. The volleyball court is located south of Qunce Hall, covering more than 10 mu. The women's sports field, located south of Qunying Hall, has two tennis courts, one basketball court, and one volleyball court. The northwest corner of Qunying Hall has two tennis courts and one basketball court. There are also various other sports equipment.

The above is a glimpse of the current state of the university. Due to space limitations, it is not exhaustive. We recall that ten years ago, at the beginning of the university's founding, the roads were rough and the buildings were rudimentary, and there were countless difficulties. Now, the school buildings have been renovated, and the atmosphere is completely new. Reflecting on the past and thinking about the present, we are truly gratified! However, university education is a difficult and heavy responsibility. The university's current construction is only the beginning, and the goal of success is still far away. On the occasion of this tenth anniversary celebration, in addition to rejoicing and being encouraged, we must maintain the spirit of cooperation between teachers and students in the past and strive to promote university affairs in the future.

Great China University's Future Development Direction

— Ou Yuanhuai

Great China University, which was painstakingly managed through the cooperation of teachers and students, has now been born for ten years. Those with knowledge of its contributions to society and the nation will have a fair judgment, which need not be elaborated upon. However, looking back over the past ten years, thanks to the support and assistance of people from all walks of life and the efforts of all teachers and students, university affairs have progressed by leaps and bounds. The number of students has increased dramatically, from 200 to over 2,000; the campus has been relocated five times, and the scale has become even larger, from having no place to stand to owning 300 mu of land; the school buildings have gone from a few low houses to wide buildings connected to the clouds; 1,500 graduates are serving in various provinces and cities in China and the Nanyang Islands, and more than 100 have studied abroad, with outstanding achievements, which are visible to all. While this may not be considered to have reached the ultimate goal, it is still satisfactory and somewhat comforting to those who care about Great China University. As one of the founders and having assisted in university administration for many years, I dare not fail to discuss the plans for future development on the occasion of this tenth anniversary. However, planning is not difficult, implementation is difficult. Many plans in the past have not been realized, either due to financial constraints or lack of talent. Therefore, today, I will not aim too high but only briefly describe the most urgent constructions, for the reference of those who care about Great China University's affairs, and also as a compass for self-vigilance.

A. Regarding Future Policy Guidelines

Administrative facilities are valuable in facilitating teaching. While the university's administration has achieved many special achievements in recent years, there are still some shortcomings that do not meet the ideal. The current plan is to build on past strengths and find ways to make up for the deficiencies. Specifically, there are the following four points that should be paid attention to and implemented.

(1) Strive for Administrative Rationalization

For daily administration and all development plans, scientific methods should be used to conduct careful investigations and designs in advance, establish administrative calendars for each department, and implement them on schedule to improve efficiency. Departmental reports should also be implemented to achieve mutual supervision. In particular, as the university's finances are not very generous, all administrative expenses must strictly adhere to a policy of austerity to reduce unnecessary waste, directly reduce the school's burden, and indirectly increase educational effectiveness. At the same time, intelligence, morality, physical education, group activities, and aesthetics should be developed equally. No matter how important the facilities are, detailed plans and descriptions must be prepared and submitted to the university affairs meeting for review, in order to gather wisdom and expand benefits and give full play to the functions of the meeting system. Even students' suggestions for improving university affairs should be adopted within the realm of possibility.

(2) Maintain the Spirit of Hard Work

This university is a private school. The most formidable enemy of private schools can be summed up in one word: economic pressure. However, the birth of this university is to strive to cultivate talents for the country and to work hard for academic construction, maintaining the spirit of hard work from day to day for ten years. There is no need to worry about financial difficulties, and there is no need to fear the harsh environment. Each time we encounter danger, this spirit becomes stronger and stronger, and we are finally able to safely navigate the stormy seas. This is none other than the result of the spirit of hard work. Although the university's foundation has been established, it is still far from our ideal. In the future, all teachers and students should not only uphold the spirit of sacrifice, struggle, perseverance, and progress, but also carry it forward and make it greater. Teachers should teach diligently, staff should work diligently, and students should study diligently. With concerted efforts, we should cultivate a study style of "unceasing self-improvement" and hard work, temper its edge, and advocate it to schools across the country. From ten years, twenty years, fifty years, one hundred years, to even a thousand years, we will make "new things emerge from the grindstone" become the permanent school motto of our university.

Qunxian Hall (Large Lecture Hall)

(3) Strive for Teacher-Student Cooperation

Since its founding, our university has paid attention to teacher-student cooperation. We strive to make the entire university environment like a family between fathers, sons, brothers, and sisters. Teachers cooperate with students, teachers cooperate with teachers, and students cooperate with students. Whether it is improving university affairs, consulting on opinions, exploring academics, or solving problems, we all treat each other with sincerity. There is no deceit, and we abandon the small self to achieve the greater self, like the fusion of water and milk. We only see proactive suggestions and never hear negative criticisms. Therefore, university affairs can develop rapidly and become more and more perfect. However, the mission of university education is solemn, and future construction is still in progress. All our teachers and students should continue to work hard in accordance with the principle of "many voices make a city," and never lose sight of it. Regarding the university's current facilities and future improvement plans, we should not shirk our responsibility. Under the principle of maintaining the university itself, we should contribute our opinions and work together to promote progress. Only then can group life be maintained without decay, and the future of the university will be further developed and magnified. This is the awareness we should have and the further efforts that need to be made.

Qunce Hall (One of the Men's Dormitories)

(4) Establish Close Ties with Society

The university is society, and education is life. "Building a cart behind closed doors, its wheels will not fit the ruts," this is what the ancients warned against and what today's educators should pay close attention to. In the past, our university focused on internal consolidation and was somewhat lacking in contact with society. The current plan is to pay attention to social ties in many ways. There are four ways to establish ties: (1) Demonstrate with practical achievements and win social sympathy. (2) Connect with parents. Combined investigations and interviews, regularly report the university's situation and the student's academic performance to their family in writing; and solicit suggestions for improvement in all aspects, in order to achieve the effectiveness of cooperation between school education and family education. (3) Unite alumni. Conduct a detailed survey of their service in society, as a compass for facility construction; and make full use of school publications to communicate alumni news at any time, and introduce appropriate occupations, guide or solve their difficult problems as much as possible. (4) Serve the community. Establish a department for inquiries on social and scientific issues, and make full use of the Great China People's Education Experimental Zone facilities and methods, leading nearby people to improve crops, build hospitals and roads, and run all public welfare undertakings. At the same time, lead students to enthusiastically participate in social culture and national salvation movements, training their skills on the one hand and improving their service spirit on the other.

B. Regarding Material Construction Plans

Material construction is still an important plan for our university today. However, what we should strive for at present is to continue the unfinished work of the past, complete the basic construction and equipment, and not take a luxurious and extravagant approach. This aspect can also be divided into the following two items:

(1) Complete Basic Construction

Our university's current classrooms and dormitories are quite magnificent and solid. This season, three new middle school buildings have been built and a science hall has been expanded. The atmosphere along the Fanwangdu Pier is completely new. In the next three to five years, classrooms and science laboratories should be sufficient. However, due to economic limitations, a general office has not been built separately, and it is temporarily located downstairs in Qunxian Hall. Recently, the number of students has increased, and various research laboratories have been established one after another, and it feels that it is not enough to allocate. Furthermore, a permanent library and a covered playground are still lacking, which is particularly regrettable. The above construction is of utmost importance to administrative efficiency and teaching and training. We hope that the board of trustees and all teachers and students will work hard to plan and work together to promote progress. Based on past history, it should not be difficult to complete this mission in a short period of time.

(2) Enrich Various Equipment

The university is a research institution for higher learning. It is not only about attending classes and copying notes, but also about paying attention to extracurricular reading and experimentation. However, to engage in large-scale experimental research, the university's current books and instruments are still insufficient. In addition to continuing to expand the designated funds each year, it is planned to hold a donation campaign in the shortest possible time. In addition, the addition of sports equipment and the expansion of sanitary facilities should be actively planned and implemented as soon as possible. As for the two major book bureaus, Commercial Press and Chung Hwa Book Company, which are permanently lending various precious books, instruments, specimens, and models, totaling more than 5,000 items, and the Educational Museum's History and Geography Social Research Office compiling newspaper indexes, are all solid research work and are worth expanding and striving for.

C. Regarding Teaching and Guidance Improvement Policies

Chinese people often have a wrong idea that middle and primary schools should pay more attention to teaching and training, and that universities are free to study and research, and there is no need to investigate teaching methods. Training is even more irrelevant. As a result, professors often teach their books, and students are at a loss to understand the profoundness. The study style is weak and discouraged, and the floating and romantic phases are followed as usual. Those who can self-restrain, struggle, and work hard are rare and cannot be seen more often. Is there any hope for a bright future for academic prospects! Therefore, the improvement of teaching and guidance is an urgent task that cannot be delayed. The main points are described below.

(1) Establish Teaching Guidelines

Teaching should have guidelines so that there is something to follow and not to aim at nothing. The university should establish teaching guidelines in the future: (1) Each subject should focus on promoting national revival, and all courses should have systematic connections. (2) The compilation of teaching materials should be based on localism, striving to meet the needs of the national conditions, and be knowledge and skills that are in line with modern life. (3) Use various excellent teaching methods to implement rigorous training, in order to increase educational efficiency and improve students' level. (4) Pay attention to health education to train the body and mind of young people. (5) Cultivate the spirit of struggle and creation.

(2) Strive for Production Education

Production education is of utmost importance to the enrichment of national livelihoods and the revitalization of rural education. Furthermore, the western suburbs of Shanghai are vast and the villages are densely populated, and there are many resources that can be used. The university plans to add agricultural and industrial colleges in the near future. This season, a production education teacher training class will be added to the College of Education to train teachers for vocational supplementary schools and labor teachers for primary and secondary schools. Currently, all plans and courses are being drafted in detail, and a preparatory committee has been organized to conduct large-scale discussions on production education, as a basis for national revival. We hope that all teachers and students will work hard to promote it!

(3) Promote Universal Physical Education

The strength of the physique is of utmost importance to the rise and fall of the nation. However, the common problem of general universities in recent years is to focus on competition and ignore the physical training of the majority of students, so that young people do not like sports and their spirits are weak. In order to promote universal physical education this season, the university has greatly expanded the sports field and sports equipment, and stipulates that morning exercises and extracurricular sports are compulsory courses for all students, and provides different training according to their abilities, genders, and seasons. We must ensure that each student has the opportunity to properly exercise their body, in order to cultivate a healthy physique and establish a foundation for the revival of China.

(4) Implement Cooperative Training and Teaching

Our university has always advocated cooperative training and teaching. The implementation of the mentor system dates back six years, which was the beginning of universities nationwide. Over the years, it has been quite effective. Starting this semester, the original system will be improved. All students in each college of the university and the teachers' special courses will be arranged in groups according to their major and minor departments, and more than 30 mentors will be assigned to provide practical guidance. The guidance period is from the student's enrollment to graduation; the scope is roughly divided into self-study, autonomy, health, and social service; the methods, in addition to not violating the principles of training and the university's school motto, can be freely determined by the mountain instructor, and the form is not limited: the mentor can make an appointment for group or individual talks with each student, or the student can raise personal questions at any time and ask the mentor. We must implement the new life in order to nurture a sound central idea and prepare for serving society and the country in the future. This is also one of the ends of reviving national education.

(5) Promote Academic Creation

Our university is one of the highest institutions of learning in the country, and with the New Culture Movement as its background, it should cultivate a atmosphere of academic research and be a model for general universities. In the future, the university should actively expand books and instruments, add various research laboratories, hold academic lectures, and increase scholarship funds, in order to promote research spirit, stimulate creative psychology, pay attention to extracurricular experiments, and encourage topic research. Teachers should also redouble their efforts in imparting social knowledge and training scientific skills, and pay attention to identifying geniuses at any time, in order to create outstanding leaders. However, the promotion of external forces is ultimately not as good as the power of internal self-initiation. The last hope is that all students will firmly focus on their interests, grasp their self-confidence, and thoroughly and eternally explore, impartially evaluate, with a calm mind, an open heart, sharp eyes, and agile hands, on their special subjects. Only then can they integrate and understand, and things will come naturally. True knowledge and practical learning cannot be overthrown. This kind of research spirit is the lifeblood of the university, and it is also what cultivates great thinkers, great inventors, great scientists, and great entrepreneurs.

One of the Library Reading Rooms

(6) Nurture a Sound Personality

University students are the backbone of society and are responsible for building the country. While the cultivation of the spirit of academic research is important on weekdays, the nurturing of a sound personality is even more indispensable. We carefully observe the accumulated ills of today's society and the degradation of general university students, and believe that the goals of implementing personality education today are: first, to advocate integrity and be indifferent to power and profit; second, to be responsible and abide by the law; third, to be disciplined and practice the new life; fourth, to be diligent and frugal and endure hardship; fifth, to be clear about etiquette and righteousness and be honest and self-respecting. We must enable young students to wake up in time and fiercely prescribe medicine on the work of cultivating themselves and controlling themselves, to completely wash away the bad habits of past floating, romantic, frivolous, extravagant, and luxurious, to cultivate a beautiful and pure academic style, to establish a clean and healthy life, to maintain the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation, to clearly distinguish between righteousness and profit, to identify right and wrong, to hone their ambitions, and to adhere to their integrity. They must be like this in haste, and they must be like this in adversity. They will be like this from morning to night, and they will not be sloppy in the slightest. The way to advance morality and cultivate character is here, and the way to build achievements and establish a career is also here!

As the saying goes: "It is easy to share adversity, but difficult to share prosperity." Although the development of our university to this point cannot be said to have reached the realm of "prosperity," it has certainly entered the path of "modest prosperity." We hope that all teachers and students will always remember the ancient poem "The wind and rain are dark, the rooster crows incessantly," and encourage each other with "unceasing self-improvement," taking another step forward on a hundred-foot pole, sincerely understanding the glory of the past, hoping for the progress of the future, working hard to study and exercise, cultivating leading talents, and promoting the national spirit, in order to complete the mission of university education. This is what Yuanhuai should serve with utmost dedication, and it also depends on the efforts of all teachers and students.

The Implementation of the Universal Mentor System at Great China University

— Lu Jizeng

1. The Significance of the Mentor System

The purpose of the mentor system is to rationalize the relationship between teachers and students. The poor relationship between teachers and students in schools today is the cause of the decline of education in our country. If we want to save this chaotic world, we must start by creating a new educational ethic. The mentor system is a special attempt to create this new ethic.

The quality of the study style is the responsibility of all staff and students. Although the causes of the ups and downs of student movements are extremely complex, the abnormal state between teachers and students is a credible explanation. The fact that teachers are not like teachers and students are not like students is the main cause of student movements.

One of the Chemistry Laboratories

The "Teacher's Discourse" by Han Yu says: "A teacher is one who imparts the Way, imparts knowledge, and resolves doubts." Only those who can fulfill this responsibility can be called a great mentor. Because a mentor embodies the three meanings of "teacher," "beneficial friend," and "guide." In ancient times, visiting teachers and befriending them was considered essential for establishing oneself. Today's students who wish to gain a good teacher must first have sincere respect for the teacher and value the Way; those who wish to gain a beneficial friend must first have a heart of trustworthiness, righteousness, and loyalty; those who wish to seek a mentor with outstanding insight must first have the enthusiasm to immerse themselves in truth and strive for excellence. Mentors should engage in academic discussions with such students to enlighten their wisdom, temper their morality to cultivate their personality, and collaborate on planning the foundations of their careers to encourage their courage and ambition in their professions.

Education for the revitalization of the nation must supplement classroom instruction with character education and vocational guidance in order to fully realize the functions of the school. Now, the mentor uses their qualifications as a teacher to impart essential knowledge to students, shapes students' emotions with their identity as a beneficial friend, and cultivates students' aspirations with their position as a guide, so that students' intelligence, benevolence, and courage all reach the highest level, and their knowledge, emotions, and will are fully integrated into their actions. If students are promising talents and not willing to abandon themselves, then this kind of education will not only be comparable to Rousseau's "Emile" but will also lay the foundation for national revival. Now, I will further explain my humble opinion with a simple diagram as follows:

2. The Process of Implementing the Mentorship System in Our School

Since the founding of our school in the 13th year of the Republic of China, it has been rich in the true spirit of the mentorship system. Teachers and students have shared weal and woe, united in their efforts in the reading movement to establish this brand-new institution. The glory of cooperation between teachers and students in our school has long been a popular story in the history of education at home and abroad. The implementation of the mentorship system in our school can be divided into the following four periods in terms of time: the first is the period of having the substance without the name, which can also be called the beginning period, that is, the three years from the autumn of the 13th year of the Republic of China to the autumn of the 16th year. During this period, the central professors were all rich in the spirit of mentorship, and the students were all rich in the ambition to accept instruction. Therefore, the whole school was not only full of the remnants of ancient academies but also had the practical effect of a school family. The second is the reform and innovation period, that is, from the autumn of the 16th year of the Republic of China to the autumn of the 21st year. In these five years, the whole body of teachers and students of our school painstakingly and with great effort, the system of mentorship, the outline is well-ordered. But we were still not confident that it was completely proper at that time, so we adopted an experimental attitude and only implemented it in the fourth-year undergraduate students and the second-year teacher training students who were about to graduate. The third is the expansion period, that is, from the autumn of the 21st year to the autumn of the 23rd year. In these two years, we took the courage gained from experience, in addition to the special graduating class students of the undergraduate and teacher training programs, we also added all the first-year undergraduate students and the freshman students of the psychology department. The number of students being mentored increased several times compared to before, and the number of mentors also increased greatly. The fourth is the universalization period. That is, from the beginning of this semester. In short, the mentorship system in our school has a history of ten years. We regard it as no less than a tree planted by our generation, which has reached the stage of containing buds and wanting to bloom. Now, I will further explain the late transformation of the mentorship system in our school with a simple diagram.

First Period—Gestation Period—Autumn of the 13th Year of the Republic to Autumn of the 16th Year—Experimented on undergraduate students and teacher training students about to graduate

Third Period—Expansion Period—Autumn of the 21st Year to Autumn of the 23rd Year—Added all freshmen of the undergraduate and teacher training programs

Fourth Period—Universalization Period—Starting from this semester, universalized to all students in the school

3. Overview of the Implementation of the Universalized Mentorship System in This Semester

Since the implementation of the universalized mentorship system is an important part of our school's education for national rejuvenation, its intention was actually far back in the autumn of last year. After careful planning by the National Rejuvenation Education Committee and repeated discussions by the school's school affairs meetings, its nine articles of regulations were passed at the 160th school affairs meeting. Then, at the 161st school affairs meeting, its eleven articles of implementation details were passed. Therefore, the rules and regulations for the mentorship system determined this time were not hastily drawn up, but were carefully planned based on past experience, current needs, and future trends. The scope of its implementation is from partial to universal to all students, and the selection of mentors is based on the school's employment of professors who have a close relationship with the students' department, and the period of guidance is from the time of enrollment to the time of leaving the school, all belonging to the same mentor, and no changes may be made in the middle. A mentor meeting is held once a month to report on the progress of each person's guidance and to discuss all issues related to guidance. Currently, the school has appointed a total of thirty-three mentors, each mentoring from thirty to fifty students. Since the beginning of guidance, it has been very active. To discuss it further, today's method has many advantages over the past: First, the universalization of implementation. Students of all levels can enjoy the benefits of mentor guidance, not just limited to the highest or lowest grades, causing students in other grades to feel regret. Second, it is convenient for academic research. All designated mentors have a close relationship with the students' chosen departments; they share the same views, and those who are being guided can ask for advice and take in the essence day and night. To make attempts to reach the peak; and those who are mentors can display their strengths and do their best to guide, and the insights and accumulations they have gained from their diligent work in normal times can be passed on to others, so that academics will become more prosperous and brilliant day by day. Otherwise, if the professor who has no close relationship with the students' research is their mentor, because of different interests, students will inevitably suffer the pain of going in the opposite direction if they want to do further research. Third, it is suitable for life guidance. The mentor's guidance for students, in addition to oral instruction and written description, the most important thing is the mentor's great personality, which enlightens students and allows them to receive excellent guidance unknowingly, so that they can be included within the orbit of things. If mentors are changed frequently, and the period of guidance is very short, students cannot have a deep understanding of the mentor, how can they get excellent hints and produce satisfactory reflections! Conversely, mentors must also have long-term and clear observations of students before they can have correct and appropriate guidance, which is by no means possible with a short period of guidance. Now, our school stipulates that students should follow the same mentor from the time they enter the school to the time they leave the school, then students will spend years in school with their mentor, and their feelings will become closer day by day. Not only can the mentor have a clear observation of the student and give correct guidance, but the student can also receive the mentor's personality cultivation, like bathing in timely rain, like sitting in the spring breeze, and unconsciously being induced to become excellent talents. The greatness of its effect can be asserted.

Qunyingzhai (Girls' Dormitory)

The Process of Constructing New School Buildings for Daxia Middle School

— Ni Wenya

Our school was founded in the autumn of the 14th year of the Republic of China, only one year after the establishment of Daxia University. With the entire foundation of Daxia not yet stable, the situation of our school can be imagined. The initial classrooms were the Pan Clan Ancestral Hall on Binlang Road, and the newest dormitory was No. 201 Xiaoshadu Road. In the autumn of the second year, No. 15 Singapore Road was rented as a school building. In the spring of the 16th year, British soldiers gathered in Shanghai, and the school building was suddenly occupied; it was necessary to move back to No. 201 Xiaoshadu Road. In the autumn of the same year, it was merged into the university school building on Jiaozhou and Yuezhou Roads, so as to save expenses. In the spring of the 17th year, No. 88 Gordon Road was rented as a school meeting place; in the autumn, No. 131 Gordon Road was rented as the second academy. In the autumn of the 19th year, the university department was completed in the new school building on Zhongshan Road, so the original school building on Jiaozhou Road was completely taken over by our school for application. After the January 28th Incident in the 21st year, the university department moved back to Jiaozhou Road again; the two departments of the university and the middle school were in the same place for half a year. From the autumn of that year, our school moved into the university school building on Zhongshan Road—the original auditorium was converted into the general office of the two departments of the university and the middle school, and part of Qunxian Hall was used as classrooms for our school, and the male and female students lived separately in Qunli and Qunying dormitories. It was like this for two years.

Originally, the middle school attached to the university has something that ordinary middle schools cannot reach: First, there is an opportunity to use the library equipment of the university. Second, there are more opportunities to get knowledge outside of class. Third, it is easy to arouse the desire to study academic knowledge, and even students who did not work hard in school became diligent. Fourth, admission to higher education can avoid departments that do not fit one's interests and abilities, and admission to higher education is equal to promotion. Fifth, there are more personal and group contacts, and there will be more opportunities for mutual assistance and cooperation when serving the society in the future. However, only this relatively strong academic atmosphere can be used to induce and increase the desire and opportunity for middle school students to study. As for the exploration of knowledge and the method of guidance, it must be rich in the color of secondary education; and all student life must conform to the norms of middle school student life. This principle is the dividing line between the success and failure of all university-affiliated middle schools. If you can't grasp this principle, then the advantages of the university-affiliated middle school cannot be obtained, and the disadvantages that ordinary middle schools do not have are there. If you want to grasp this principle, you have to rely on the efforts of the middle school faculty; but teaching, training, and school building facilities are closely related. It is not good to have form without spirit, but it is also difficult to just hope for spirit without form. For example, in mixed canteens, dormitories, lounges, classrooms, and the same schedule, the color of middle school is difficult to encourage. In school buildings where university and middle school students are mixed, it is at least twice the effort to implement middle school student life guidance that is different from that of universities. The situation of our school's relocation of school buildings before the summer of the 21st year was like a picture of a refugee republic. Since the autumn of the 21st year, we have always hoped that the independent middle school building will be realized as soon as possible, which will be beneficial without harm.

Library

This year, in the spring, this ideal gradually became concrete. The drawings of the new school building were drawn by Mr. Liu Shimo, director of the civil engineering department of our school's high school, and the construction was contracted by Juechuan Construction Factory, a graduate of our school. The construction was supervised by Mr. Zhang Xingke and other two graduates of the current civil engineering department of our school's high school. Construction started in early May and was fully completed after more than four months to September. There is one office building, with the middle school director's office, the teaching office, the general office, the teacher's lounge, the reception room, and the conference room on the ground floor; a large library and a reading room on the upper floor, which can accommodate more than one hundred students. There are two classroom buildings, with sixteen ordinary classrooms, one physics and chemistry classroom, and one labor classroom, as well as one sports department and one Boy Scout headquarters. The north side of the new school building is also used as a morning exercise field and various sports fields. Male and female students still live separately in Qunli and Qunying dormitories, and are separated from the university by various means.

New School Building of Daxia Middle School (One of the Classrooms)

Since the establishment of our school in the 14th year, it has been exactly ten years. During these ten years, the internal and external troubles encountered by the country have caused the entire nation to feel extremely shaken psychologically and in life. Our school has uniquely received enthusiastic support from people in the society and harmonious cooperation between teachers and students in the school, so that both spiritual and material aspects have made considerable progress. I sincerely hope that all colleagues and all students will cherish the difficulty of the past and work together to realize a more glorious future!

One of the New School Buildings of the Affiliated Daxia Middle School—Office

Sports News

Four American Track and Field Athletes Performed in Shenyuan Yesterday, the Skills of Famous Athletes are Indeed Extraordinary

Mr. Deng's Shot Put and Discus Results are Amazing

Others Tried Their Skills in Inverted Events

The first-class American track and field athletes, who set off from the United States this autumn and traveled to the east, performed in Japan. Among the sixteen people in the country, eight returned to the United States, and the remaining eight performed in Shanghai and the Philippines, and returned from the Philippines to the north. Four people, including Mutuogafu, went to Europe via Hong Kong, and four people, including Keyinhai, Crowle, and Deng, came to Shanghai from Hong Kong. They were invited by the Chinese National Sports Association to perform. The four people, including Keyinhai, arrived here on the Japanese ship Asama Maru at 10:30 yesterday morning. They landed at the Huishan Wharf. Shen Siliang and Xi Qingtuo of the Sports Association also came to the pier to welcome them. The group of seven went to Xi Qing to have lunch with Shen and others. In the afternoon at three o'clock, they drove to Shenyuan to perform. More than a thousand people who heard the news came to watch, hoping to see the champions of the world sports arena. The American School of Shanghai also planned to invite the four athletes to perform at the school this morning, but they all politely declined because of the tight schedule. They decided to take the original ship stationed in Shanghai back to the United States at 10:30 this morning. The performance yesterday is recorded as follows,

100 meters (1) Green (USA) 11.6 seconds, (2) Cheng Jinkuan (3) Wu Ci (Shanghai American) (4) Pei Yuan (Shanghai English)

200 meters Green (USA·33 seconds 2, (2) Cheng Jinkuan, (3) Wu Ci (Shanghai American) (4) Pei Yuan (Shanghai English)

400 meters (1) Keyinhai (USA) 53.8 seconds, (2) Hugh Tuo (Shanghai English), (3) Teng Geer (Shanghai American), (4) Fang Xijie (Shanghai English) Our country did not participate,

800 meters (1) Keyinhai (USA) 2 minutes 12 seconds 2, (2) Jia Daren, (3) Adams (Shanghai American),

3000 meters (1) Crowe (USA) 9 minutes 35 seconds, (2) Wang Zhenglin 10 minutes 8 seconds 2, (3) Jin Zhongkang,

Shot Put Mr. Deng (USA) 15 meters 19 (breaking the Far East's highest record of 12 meters 905), (2) Walker (Shanghai American), (3) Shen Weishen,

Discus (1) Mr. Deng (USA) 47 meters 83, (breaking the Far East's highest record of 42 meters 545), (2) Hawkes (Shanghai American),

1000 meters relay (1) American athletes, 0 minutes 2 minutes 14 seconds, (2) Mixed team,

Mr. Deng's Shot Put Posture (Photo by Ye Changlie)

Not Fully Exercised

Yesterday, the four athletes only slightly showed their skills, and they did not use their full strength in the inverted events. Except for Crowle, all those who ran were not their strengths. For example, Keyinhai is the one who set new world records in the 1,500 meters and 1 mile,

Yesterday he ran 400 meters and 800 meters, Green is good at 400 meters, but yesterday he ran 100 meters and 200 meters, and Keyinhai was suffering from a cold, and he came to the field sick, because he could not refuse the kindness. Crowe is the one who set a new world record in the 3,000 meters, and Mr. Deng is good at iron balls and iron cakes. Because no one competed with him, the records were not particularly outstanding.

Speaking from Experience

Among the four people, Keyinhai and Green have the best starting and running posture, relaxed and with big steps. Before the performance, according to Keyinhai, sports are also related to talent. Even in long-distance running, the world's long-distance running is always not as good as Finland. The training methods of other countries are no worse than Finland, but they cannot compare with Finland, which is also a strange thing. Japan has indeed made great progress and effort, but there is no shortage of talent. Keyinhai started training at the age of seven. When he was at the University of Kansas, he saved his brother from a fire, and his feet were severely burned by the fire. Fortunately, he was well taken care of and was able to practice again. Keyinhai showed his feet, which were full of scars, and he still did not feel completely healed. Mr. Deng also elaborated on the method of throwing a shot put, how to exert force, and how to throw it, saying that his own force is entirely in the thrust of the waist.

A Shoulder's Difference

The 100 meters was the first event. Green, the 400-meter athlete, inverted the series. After the American Lanhuo fired the gun, the Chinese athlete Cheng Jinkuan took the lead all the way, and the limelight was very strong. Green pressed hard from behind. At the last 15 meters, Green jumped forward. At the finish line, Cheng lost by a shoulder. Green's score was only 11.6 seconds. In the 200 meters, Green took the lead all the way, and Cheng Jinkuan was always behind. At the finish line, Green won by five meters, and the score was 23.2 seconds. Cheng was very depressed yesterday, I don't know why.

Came to the Field Sick

Keyinhai suffered from a cold and came to the field sick yesterday because he could not refuse the kindness. He first ran 800 meters, then 400 meters. Chinese athletes did not participate in the 400 meters. Keyinhai's score of 53.8 seconds was not his strength. In the 800 meters, China's Xu Lianren and Adams ran together. In the first 500 meters, Keyinhai always followed in the middle, seemingly to increase interest and not want to put people too far behind. In the 300 meters after 500 meters, Keyinhai began to speed up, and at the finish line, he dropped Jia Lianren by 60 meters. The score was 2 minutes 12 seconds 2. Keyinhai ran this item without taking off his trousers and coat. His steps were loose and big, and the movements of his hands were good, and his posture was beautiful.

(Top) Crowle (Bottom) Green (Photo by Wang Kai)

3000 Meters

Wang Zhenglin and Jin Zhongkang ran together. After the gun was fired, Wang followed closely behind Crowle, not letting go of a step. For the first 1,000 meters, Wang and Crowle were inseparable. Jin Zhongkang gradually fell behind and had no chance to catch up. After 1,000 meters, Crowle's pace accelerated, and Wang began to fall behind. A total of seven laps of rice. At 1,500 meters, Wang was 20 meters behind, and when he reached the finish line, Wang was 200 meters behind. Crowle's score was 9 minutes 35 seconds, which is far from the world record. Wang Zhenglin's score was 10 minutes 8 seconds 2, which also did not break the national record.

Amazing Distance

Mr. Deng performed shot put and discus, and his burly figure made people amazed. His weight should be more than 250 pounds. Compared with our country's Chen Tieniu, he is just a small wizard meeting a big wizard. His ankles are also small, so his elasticity is abundant. The shot put thrown by him is very high in the air, so the landing point is far away. His second throw was 15 meters 19. The other two people, Shen Weishen only got 9 meters 88, and Walker reached more than 10 meters. After the discus was released from Mr. Deng's hand, it flew away, and the whole field was amazed. It was 47 meters 83, exceeding the Far East record by more than five meters.

Mixed Relay

Finally, in the twilight, a 1,000-meter relay race with different distances was held. The first person ran 100 meters, the second person ran 200 meters, the third person ran 300 meters, and the fourth person ran 400 meters. The order of the American athletes was (1) Mr. Deng, (2) Keyinhai (3) Crowle (4) Green, the order of the Shanghai mixed team was (1) Wang Jihuai, (2) Gai Boman, (3) Hugh Tuo, (4) Fang Xijie, the American team won with a score of 2 minutes 14 seconds.

Educational News

Shanghai Universities Jointly Implement Measures to Strictly Prohibit Students from Entering Dance Halls

Cooperating with the Municipal Government to Dispatch Police Officers to Patrol Dance Halls

Guiding Students to Develop a Sense of Automatic Abstinence

Since the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Universities Joint Association resolved on the 27th to strictly prohibit students from entering dance halls, it has aroused considerable attention in academic circles and sympathy in public opinion. A reporter from the *Fu Xin* News Agency made a special visit to an executive committee member of the University Association yesterday to inquire about the implementation measures of the case. It is said that dancing is a legitimate entertainment and is regarded as a necessary skill in social circles in European and American countries. However, the purpose of dancing in our country's dance halls is quite different. It misleads young people and greatly hinders students' studies. Therefore, there was a resolution to strictly prohibit students from entering dance halls. At that time, the method of implementation was discussed. It was decided to send a letter to the Municipal Government of this city to cooperate in handling the matter. The Municipal Government will send police officers to patrol various dance halls in rotation. If students are found dancing in the hall, they will be arrested immediately. A reply has now been received from the Municipal Government agreeing to assist. As for the University Association itself, it will also work with various schools to send personnel to inspect the dance halls day and night. If students are found, their names will be recorded and reported to the school, and they will be expelled without leniency. On the other hand, students in various schools will be guided to develop a sense of automatically abstaining from entering dance halls.

The Municipal Botanical Garden, Prepared for Many Years, Officially Opens

Located at the Former Site of the Gezhi Academy on Longhua Road

Beautifully Positioned with Flowers, Trees, and Fruit Trees

In addition to the zoo established by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education on Wenmiao Road in the Nanshi area, which has already been opened, a botanical garden has also been established at the intersection of Longhua Road and Xinqiao Road. After a year of preparation, it has now been completed and officially opened on October 1st. A reporter from the *Shanghai News* made a special trip to visit yesterday. The details of the garden are recorded as follows:

History of Construction: The establishment of a botanical garden in Shanghai is a pioneering endeavor. In 1924, the Shanghai County Bureau of Education established a public school garden near Penglai Market, at the site of the current Shangwen Elementary School. It contained both animals and plants, exclusively for the use of students from various schools as extracurricular reference material. In 1928, it was transferred to municipal control, and the content was gradually enriched. In October of last year, the Shangwen Elementary School began constructing a new school building at the site, and the public school garden was closed. The animals were moved to the municipal zoo, and all the plants were moved to the current botanical garden.

Official Opening: The garden has been under preparation since last year. The garden site is the former site of the Gezhi Academy. Repairs to the buildings, construction of flower houses, and landscaping began in August of last year. The cost was over 13,000 yuan. The Municipal Bureau of Education appointed Jiang Xi-yi as the director of the garden to actively manage it, and it officially opened on October 1st. The opening hours are from 8:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m.

Layout of the Garden: The garden occupies several acres. It is surrounded by fences, with an office, exhibition room, and research room in the center. The research room is equipped with plant classification, plant morphology forms, and specimen-making tools for students from various schools to use for experiments and reference. The exhibition room displays various plant specimens in picture frames, which is quite beautiful. Outside is the garden area, divided into five sections: practical crop area, industrial crop area, fruit tree area, forest area, and flower area. There is also a flower house, which cost 4,000 yuan to build. It is equipped with hot water pipes, and the surrounding area and roof are all glass, specially for growing tropical plants.

Welcome to Visit: The Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice yesterday stating that the municipal botanical garden at the intersection of Longhua Road and Xinqiao Road in Nanshi has been prepared by the Bureau and will officially open on November 1st. All citizens and teachers and students of public and private schools at all levels are welcome to visit freely for research purposes. In addition to reporting to the authorities and ordering it to be distributed, this is a special notice.

Ministry of Education Orders All Provincial and Municipal Departments to Forward All Middle School Textbooks to the Bureaus for Review

Since the Ministry of Education promulgated the curriculum standards, it has ordered all provincial and municipal departments to submit elementary school textbooks to the Ministry for review in accordance with the new standards and the latest departmental regulations. Currently, bookstores often only submit one volume at a time for review, failing to submit the entire set systematically. Therefore, a general order has been issued to all provincial and municipal education departments to instruct bookstores: (1) All textbooks that have already been submitted to the Ministry for review but are not complete (e.g., only the first volume has been submitted and not the second volume, or only one or two of the eight or four volumes have been submitted) must be supplemented in full when submitted for review next time. (2) All textbooks that have not been submitted for review must be submitted in full at one time in the future.

Datong University Celebrates Tenth Anniversary This Morning

Practicing the Spirit of Hard Work in Management, Teaching, and Learning

In the Future, Taking National Rejuvenation Education as the Overall Goal

Datong University has been established since the autumn of 1924, and it has now been ten years. The main goal of the university's establishment is a reading movement. All teachers and students cooperate and are extremely rich in the spirit of sacrifice, struggle, and creation. Its three tenets of hard work—hard work in management by staff, hard work in teaching by professors, and hard work in learning by students—have remained unchanged for ten years. The tenth anniversary celebration will be held at 9:00 a.m. today. A summary of the situation is provided below:

Historical Development

The university's campus has changed several times. At first, only a preparatory office was set up in a rented house in Meirenli, Bei Di-E Road, French Concession. Then, it moved to Yichang Road at the end of Gordon Road. Then, it moved to 201 Xiaoshadu Road. Then, it moved to 301 Jiaozhou Road. In the autumn of 1930, it finally moved to its magnificent new campus built on Zhongshan Road, Fanwangdu, thus laying a permanent foundation for a century of educating people. The university has long been approved for registration by the Ministry of Education and is listed among the famous universities in the country.

A Glimpse of the Current Situation

Now, the university's campus is magnificent and beautiful, all designed in the latest style. It includes a large classroom, Qunxian Hall, a boys' dormitory, Qunce Zhai, a boys' dormitory, Qunli Zhai, a girls' dormitory, Qunying Zhai, a science hall, a library, a grand auditorium, a sanatorium, three new Datong Middle School campus buildings, twelve teachers' and staff dormitories, city rooms, dining halls, bungalows, and all necessary ancillary buildings. Overlooking the entire campus, there are ancient trees, open fields, clear streams, ponds, spacious playgrounds, fresh air, and a pure environment. The layout of the Sun Yat-sen design is rich in natural scenery. The equipment in the library and science facilities is quite complete, and the establishment of the Education Hall and the Public Education Experimental Area is particularly distinctive. In total, the university currently has 1,300 university students and 600 middle school students, moving forward steadily.

Future Direction

In the future, the university's administrative policy has been decided last winter to take national rejuvenation education as the overall goal. Its efforts are directed in about four areas: (1) Strictly implement personality education to cultivate sound national morality; (2) Promote production education to save the endangered national economy; (3) Reward science education to develop the infinite natural treasures; (4) Implement national defense education to cultivate the nation's self-defense capabilities. At this time of serious national crisis, who will maintain the order? The university's spirit of struggle, sacrifice, and creation may well be the pearl for our nation to save itself and survive in the future.

Anniversary Ceremony

The tenth anniversary celebration will be held at 9:00 a.m. this morning. The mayor of the city, heads of education institutions, and presidents of various universities, including Liu Zhan-en, Li Zhao-huan, and Xiao You-mei, as well as university directors such as Du Yue-sheng, Zhang Zhu-ping, and Jiang Wen-yu, will all participate in the anniversary ceremony. At 12:00 noon, the directors, teachers, staff, and graduates will have a banquet. At 2:00 p.m., the inauguration ceremony of the new Datong Middle School campus will be held. From 4:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m., the university's graduates will hold a reunion on campus. At 6:00 p.m., there will be a lantern parade. At 8:00 p.m., spectacular fireworks will be set off. It is reported that stores on nearby Zhongshan Road will hang flags and lights in celebration. Details have been published by the university's Datong University Journal and Datong Weekly in a special tenth-anniversary issue, as well as various special publications with exquisite illustrations, which will be distributed to guests at the meeting.
